to二行nikaitearu。主人hachoxtsuto神秘的na顔woshiteshibaraku一頁wo無言nomama眺meteirunode、迷亭ha横合kara「何dai新体詩kane」to云inagara覗ki込nde「yaa、捧getane。東風君、思i切xtsute富子嬢ni捧getanohaerai」toshikirini賞meru。主人hanao不思議souni「東風san、kono富子to云unoha本当ni存在shiteiru婦人nanodesuka」to聞ku。「hee、kono前迷亭先生togoisshoni朗読会he招待shita婦人no一人desu。tsuikono御近所ni住ndeorimasu。実hatada今詩集wo見seyouto思ttechoxtsuto寄xtsute参rimashitaga、生憎先月kara大磯he避暑ni行xtsute留守deshita」to真面目kusaxtsute述beru。「苦沙弥君、korega二十世紀nandayo。sonna顔woshinaide、早ku傑作demo朗読surusa。shikashi東風君kono捧ge方ha少shimazukattane。konoaekanito云u雅言ha全体何to言u意味dato思tterukane」「蚊弱itokatayowakuto云u字dato思imasu」「naruhodosoumo取ren事hanaiga本来no字義wo云uto危u気nito云u事daze。dakara僕narakouha書kanaine」「dou書itaramoxtsuto詩的ninarimashou」「僕narakousa。世no人ni似zuaekani見e給u富子嬢no鼻no下ni捧gutosurune。wazukani三字noyukisatsudaga鼻no下gaarunotonainotodeha大変感jini相違gaaruyo」「naruhodo」to東風君ha解shikanetatokorowo無理ni納得shita体nimotenasu。
　主人ha無言nomamayouyaku一頁wohagutteiyoiyo巻頭第一章wo読mi出su。

倦njite薫zuru香裏ni君no
霊ka相思no煙notanabiki
oo我、aa我、辛kikono世ni
amaku得teshika熱ki口duke

「koreha少々僕niha解shikaneru」to主人ha嘆息shinagara迷亭ni渡su。「koreha少々振i過giteru」to迷亭ha寒月ni渡su。寒月ha「naaaruhodo」to云xtsute東風君ni返su。
「先生御分rininarannohagomottomode、十年前no詩界to今日no詩界toha見違eruhodo発達shiteorimasukara。kono頃no詩ha寝転nde読ndari、停車場de読ndehatoutei分riyouganainode、作xtsuta本人desura質問wo受keruto返答ni窮suru事gayokuarimasu。全kuinsupire-shonde書kunode詩人hasono他niha何等no責任monainodesu。註釈ya訓義ha学究noyaru事de私共no方deha頓to構imasen。sendattemo私no友人de送籍to云u男ga一夜toiu短篇wokakimashitaga、誰ga読ndemo朦朧toshite取ri留megatsukanainode、当人ni逢xtsute篤to主意noarutokorowo糺shite見tanodesuga、当人mosonna事ha知ranaiyoto云xtsute取ri合wanainodesu。全kusono辺ga詩人no特色kato思imasu」「詩人kamo知renaiga随分妙na男desune」to主人ga云uto、迷亭ga「馬鹿dayo」to単簡ni送籍君wo打chi留meta。東風君hakoredakedehamada弁ji足rinai。「送籍ha吾々仲間nouchidemo取除kedesuga、私no詩modouka心持chisono気de読ndeitadakitainode。kotoni御注意wo願itainohakarakikono世to、amaki口duketo対wotottatokoroga私no苦心desu」「yohodo苦心wonasuxtsuta痕迹ga見emasu」「amaitokaraito反照surutokoronanka十七味調唐辛子調de面白i。全ku東風君独特no伎倆de敬々服々no至rida」toshikirini正直na人womaze返shite喜ndeiru。
　主人ha何to思ttaka、fuito立xtsute書斎no方he行ttagayagate一枚no半紙wo持xtsute出tekuru。「東風君no御作mo拝見shitakara、今度ha僕ga短文wo読nde諸君no御批評wo願ou」toisasaka本気no沙汰dearu。「天然居士no墓碑銘naramou二三遍拝聴shitayo」「maa、damatteinasai。東風san、koreha決shite得意nomonodehaarimasenga、honno座興desukara聴ite下sai」「是非伺gaimashou」「寒月君motsuideni聞ki給e」「tsuidedenakutemo聴kimasuyo。長i物janaideshou」「僅々六十余字sa」to苦沙弥先生iyoiyo手製no名文wo読mi始meru。
「大和魂！　to叫nde日本人ga肺病yaminoyouna咳woshita」
「起shi得te突兀desune」to寒月君gahomeru。
「大和魂！　to新聞屋ga云u。大和魂！　to掏摸ga云u。大和魂ga一躍shite海wo渡xtsuta。英国de大和魂no演説wosuru。独逸de大和魂no芝居wosuru」
「naruhodokorya天然居士以上no作da」to今度ha迷亭先生gasori返xtsute見seru。
「東郷大将ga大和魂wo有tteiru。肴屋no銀sanmo大和魂wo有tteiru。詐偽師、山師、人殺shimo大和魂wo有tteiru」
「先生sokohe寒月mo有tteirutotsukete下sai」
「大和魂hadonnamonokato聞itara、大和魂sato答ete行ki過gita。五六間行ttekaraehento云u声ga聞koeta」
「sono一句ha大出来da。君hanakanaka文才gaarune。sorekara次no句ha」
「三角namonoga大和魂ka、四角namonoga大和魂ka。大和魂ha名前no示sugotoku魂dearu。魂dearukara常nifurafurashiteiru」
「先生daibu面白ugozaimasuga、chito大和魂ga多過gihashimasenka」to東風君ga注意suru。「賛成」to云ttanoha無論迷亭dearu。
「誰mo口nisenu者hanaiga、誰mo見tamonohanai。誰mo聞ita事haaruga、誰mo遇xtsuta者ganai。大和魂hasore天狗no類ka」
　主人ha一結杳然to云utsumoride読mi終ttaga、sasugano名文moamari短ka過girunoto、主意gadokoniarunoka分rikanerunode、三人hamadaatogaaru事to思xtsute待tteiru。ikura待tteitemo、untomo、suntomo、云wanainode、最後ni寒月ga「soregiridesuka」to聞kuto主人ha軽ku「un」to答eta。unha少shi気楽過giru。
　不思議na事ni迷亭hakono名文ni対shite、itsumonoyouniamari駄弁wo振wanakattaga、yagate向ki直xtsute、「君mo短篇wo集mete一巻toshite、soushite誰kani捧getehadouda」to聞ita。主人ha事monageni「君ni捧geteyarouka」to聴kuto迷亭ha「真平da」to答etagiri、先刻細君ni見sebirakashita鋏wochokichoki云washite爪wototteiru。寒月君ha東風君ni向xtsute「君haano金田no令嬢wo知tterunokai」to尋neru。「kono春朗読会he招待shitekara、懇意ninattesorekaraha始終交際woshiteiru。僕haano令嬢no前he出ruto、何tonaku一種no感ni打tarete、当分nouchiha詩wo作ttemo歌wo詠ndemo愉快ni興ga乗xtsute出te来ru。kono集中nimo恋no詩ga多inoha全kuaa云u異性no朋友karainsupire-shonwo受kerukaradarouto思u。sorede僕haano令嬢ni対shiteha切実ni感謝no意wo表shinakerebanarankarakono機wo利用shite、waga集wo捧geru事nishitanosa。昔shikara婦人ni親友nonaimonode立派na詩wokaitamonohanaisouda」「soukanaa」to寒月君ha顔no奥de笑inagara答eta。ikura駄弁家no寄合demosou長kuha続kanmonoto見ete、談話no火no手ha大分下火ninaxtsuta。吾輩mo彼等no変化naki雑談wo終日聞kanebanaranu義務monaikara、失敬shite庭he蟷螂wo探shini出ta。梧桐no緑wo綴ru間kara西ni傾ku日ga斑rani洩rete、幹nihatsukutsuku法師ga懸命ninaiteiru。晩hakotoniyoruto一雨kakarukamo知renai。

七

　吾輩ha近頃運動wo始meta。猫no癖ni運動nante利ita風dato一概ni冷罵shi去ru手合nichoxtsuto申shi聞keruga、sou云u人間dattetsui近年madeha運動no何者taruwo解sezuni、食xtsute寝runowo天職noyouni心得teitadehanaika。無事是貴人toka称ete、懐手woshite座布団kara腐rekakaxtsuta尻wo離sazaruwomoxtsute旦那no名誉to脂下xtsute暮shitanoha覚eteiruhazuda。運動woshirono、牛乳wo飲meno冷水wo浴birono、海no中he飛bi込meno、夏ninattara山no中he籠xtsute当分霞wo食enotokudaranu注文wo連発suruyouninattanoha、西洋kara神国he伝染shishita輓近no病気de、yaharipesuto、肺病、神経衰弱no一族to心得teiikuraida。mottomo吾輩ha去年生retabakaride、当年toxtsute一歳dakara人間gakonna病気ni罹ri出shita当時no有様ha記憶ni存shiteoran、nominarazusono砌riha浮世no風中nifuwatsuiteoranakattani相違naiga、猫no一年ha人間no十年ni懸ke合uto云ttemoyoroshii。吾等no寿命ha人間yori二倍mo三倍mo短ini係razu、sono短日月no間ni猫一疋no発達ha十分仕rutokorowomoxtsute推論suruto、人間no年月to猫no星霜wo同ji割合ni打算surunohahanahadashiki誤謬dearu。第一、一歳何ヵ月ni足ranu吾輩gakonokuraino見識wo有shiteirunodemo分rudarou。主人no第三女nadoha数e年de三tsudasoudaga、智識no発達kara云uto、iyahaya鈍imonoda。泣ku事to、寝小便wosuru事to、oppaiwo飲mu事yorihokani何nimo知ranai。世wo憂i時wo憤ru吾輩nadoni較beruto、karatawainonai者da。soredakara吾輩ga運動、海水浴、転地療養no歴史wo方寸nouchini畳mi込ndeitaxtsute毫mo驚kuni足rinai。koreshikino事womoshi驚roku者gaattanara、soreha人間to云u足no二本足rinai野呂間ni極tteiru。人間ha昔kara野呂間dearu。dearukara近頃ni至xtsute漸々運動no功能wo吹聴shitari、海水浴no利益wo喋々shite大発明noyouni考erunodearu。吾輩nadoha生renai前karasonokuraina事hachanto心得teiru。第一海水ganaze薬ninarukato云ebachoxtsuto海岸he行kebasugu分ru事janaika。anna広i所ni魚ga何疋oruka分ranaiga、ano魚ga一疋mo病気woshite医者nikakaxtsuta試shiganai。minna健全ni泳ideiru。病気wosureba、karadaga利kanakunaru。死neba必zu浮ku。soredakara魚no往生woagaruto云xtsute、鳥no薨去wo、落chiruto唱e、人間no寂滅wogoneruto号shiteiru。洋行woshite印度洋wo横断shita人ni君、魚no死nutokorowo見ta事gaarimasukato聞ite見rugaii、誰demoiieto答eruni極tteiru。sorehasou答eru訳da。ikura往復shitaxtsute一匹mo波no上ni今呼吸wo引ki取xtsuta——呼吸dehaikan、魚no事dakara潮wo引ki取ttato云wanakerebanaran——潮wo引ki取xtsute浮iteirunowo見ta者hanaikarada。ano渺々taru、ano漫々taru、大海wo日tonaku夜tonaku続kezamani石炭wo焚ite探gashitearuitemo古往今来一匹mo魚ga上gatteorantokorowomoxtsute推論sureba、魚hayohodo丈夫namononi違naito云u断案hasuguni下su事ga出来ru。sorenaranaze魚gasonnani丈夫nanokato云ebakoremata人間wo待tteshikaru後ni知razarunaride、訳hanai。sugu分ru。全ku潮水wo呑nde始終海水浴woyatteirukarada。海水浴no功能hashikaku魚ni取xtsute顕著dearu。魚ni取xtsute顕著dearu以上ha人間ni取ttemo顕著denakutehanaran。一七五〇年nidokutoru・richa-do・rasserugaburaitonno海水ni飛込meba四百四病即席全快to大袈裟na広告wo出shitanoha遅i遅ito笑ttemoyoroshii。猫toiedomo相当no時機ga到着sureba、minna鎌倉atarihe出掛kerutsumorideiru。但shi今haikenai。物niha時機gaaru。御維新前no日本人ga海水浴no功能wo味wau事ga出来zuni死ndagotoku、今日no猫haimada裸体de海no中he飛bi込mubeki機会ni遭遇shiteoran。seiteha事wo仕損nzuru、今日noyouni築地he打ccharareni行xtsuta猫ga無事ni帰宅sen間ha無暗ni飛bi込mu訳niha行kan。進化no法則de吾等猫輩no機能ga狂瀾怒濤ni対shite適当no抵抗力wo生zuruni至rumadeha——換言sureba猫ga死ndato云u代rini猫ga上gattato云u語ga一般ni使用serarurumadeha——容易ni海水浴ha出来n。
　海水浴ha追xtsute実行suru事nishite、運動dakeha取riaezuyaru事ni取ri極meta。doumo二十世紀no今日運動sennohaikanimo貧民noyoude人聞kigawarui。運動wosento、運動sennodehanai。運動ga出来nnodearu、運動wosuru時間ganainodearu、余裕ganainodato鑑定sareru。昔ha運動shitamonoga折助to笑waretagotoku、今deha運動wosenu者ga下等to見做sareteiru。吾人no評価ha時to場合ni応ji吾輩no眼玉nogotoku変化suru。吾輩no眼玉hatada小sakunattari大kikunattarisurubakaridaga、人間no品隲tokuruto真逆kasamanihikkuri返ru。hikkuri返ttemo差shi支ehanai。物niha両面gaaru、両端gaaru。両端wo叩ite黒白no変化wo同一物no上ni起kosutokoroga人間no融通nokikutokorodearu。方寸wo逆kasamanishite見ruto寸方tonarutokoroni愛嬌gaaru。天no橋立wo股倉kara覗ite見rutomata格別na趣ga出ru。sekusupiyamo千古万古sekusupiyadehatsumaranai。偶niha股倉karahamurettowo見te、君korya駄目dayokuraini云u者ganaito、文界mo進歩shinaidarou。dakara運動wowaruku云xtsuta連中ga急ni運動gashitakunaxtsute、女madegarakettowo持xtsute往来woaruki廻ttaxtsute一向不思議hanai。tada猫ga運動surunowo利ita風danadoto笑isaeshinakerebayoi。sate吾輩no運動haikanaru種類no運動kato不審wo抱ku者gaarukamo知renkara一応説明shiyouto思u。御承知nogotoku不幸nishite機械wo持tsu事ga出来n。dakarabo-rumobattomo取ri扱i方ni困窮suru。次niha金ganaikara買u訳ni行kanai。kono二tsuno源因karashite吾輩no選nda運動ha一文irazu器械nashito名dukubeki種類ni属suru者to思u。sonnara、nosonoso歩kuka、aruiha鮪no切身wo啣ete馳ke出su事to考erukamo知renga、tada四本no足wo力学的ni運動sasete、地球no引力ni順xtsute、大地wo横行surunoha、amari単簡de興味ganai。ikura運動to名gatsuitemo、主人no時々実行suruyouna、読nde字nogotoki運動hadoumo運動no神聖wo汚gasu者darouto思u。勿論tadano運動demoaru刺激no下nihayarantoha限ran。鰹節競争、鮭探shinadoha結構dagakoreha肝心no対象物gaatteno上no事de、kono刺激wo取ri去ruto索然toshite没趣味namononinatteshimau。懸賞的興奮剤ganaitosureba何ka芸noaru運動gashite見tai。吾輩hairoiro考eta。台所no廂kara家根ni飛bi上garu方、家根no天辺niaru梅花形no瓦no上ni四本足de立tsu術、物干竿wo渡ru事——korehatoutei成功shinai、竹gatsurutsuru滑bextsute爪ga立tanai。後rokara不意ni小供ni飛bitsuku事、——korehasukoburu興味noaru運動no一daga滅多niyarutohidoi目ni逢ukara、高々月ni三度kuraishika試minai。紙袋wo頭hekabuseraruru事——koreha苦shiibakaridehanahada興味no乏shii方法dearu。kotoni人間no相手gaoranto成功shinaikara駄目。次niha書物no表紙wo爪de引ki掻ku事、——koreha主人ni見付karuto必zudoyasareru危険gaarunominarazu、割合ni手先no器用bakaride総身no筋肉ga働kanai。koreraha吾輩noiwayuru旧式運動naru者dearu。新式nouchinihanakanaka興味no深inogaaru。第一ni蟷螂狩ri。——蟷螂狩riha鼠狩rihodono大運動denai代rinisorehodono危険ganai。夏no半kara秋no始mehekaketeyaru遊戯toshitehamottomo上乗nomonoda。sono方法wo云utomazu庭he出te、一匹no蟷螂wosagashi出su。時候gaiito一匹ya二匹見付ke出sunoha雑作monai。sate見付ke出shita蟷螂君no傍hehaxtsuto風wo切xtsute馳kete行ku。surutosuwakosoto云u身構woshite鎌首wofuri上geru。蟷螂demonakanaka健気namonode、相手no力量wo知ranuchiha抵抗surutsumorideirukara面白i。振ri上geta鎌首wo右no前足dechoxtsuto参ru。振ri上geta首ha軟kaikaragunyari横he曲ru。kono時no蟷螂君no表情gasukoburu興味wo添eru。oyato云u思i入rega充分aru。tokorowo一足飛bini君no後rohe廻xtsute今度ha背面kara君no羽根wo軽ku引ki掻ku。ano羽根ha平生大事ni畳ndearuga、引ki掻ki方ga烈shiito、paxtsuto乱rete中kara吉野紙noyouna薄色no下着gaarawareru。君ha夏demo御苦労千万ni二枚重nede乙ni極matteiru。kono時君no長i首ha必zu後roni向ki直ru。aru時ha向ttekuruga、大概no場合niha首dakenuxtsuto立tete立tteiru。kocchikara手出shiwosurunowo待chi構ete見eru。先方gaitsumademokono態度deiteha運動ninarankara、amari長kunarutomatachoito一本参ru。koredake参ruto眼識noaru蟷螂nara必zu逃ge出su。sorewo我無洒落ni向ttekurunohayohodo無教育na野蛮的蟷螂dearu。moshi相手gakono野蛮na振舞woyaruto、向xtsute来tatokorowo覘isumashite、iyato云uhodo張ri付keteyaru。大概ha二三尺飛basareru者dearu。shikashi敵gaotonashiku背面ni前進suruto、kocchiha気no毒dakara庭no立木wo二三度飛鳥nogotoku廻ttekuru。蟷螂君hamada五六寸shika逃ge延biteoran。mou吾輩no力量wo知ttakara手向iwosuru勇気hanai。tada右往左往he逃ge惑unomidearu。shikashi吾輩mo右往左往he追kkakerukara、君hashimainiha苦shigaxtsute羽根wo振xtsute一大活躍wo試miru事gaaru。元来蟷螂no羽根ha彼no首to調和shite、sukoburu細長ku出来上gattamonodaga、聞ite見ruto全ku装飾用dasoude、人間no英語、仏語、独逸語nogotoku毫mo実用nihanaran。dakara無用no長物wo利用shite一大活躍wo試mitatokoroga吾輩ni対shiteamari功能noariyou訳ganai。名前ha活躍daga事実ha地面no上wo引kizuttearukuto云uni過gin。kounaruto少々気no毒na感haaruga運動notamedakara仕方ganai。御免蒙ttetachimachi前面he馳ke抜keru。君ha惰性de急廻転ga出来naikarayahariyamuwo得zu前進shitekuru。sono鼻wonaguritsukeru。kono時蟷螂君ha必zu羽根wo広getamama仆reru。sono上wounto前足de抑ete少shiku休息suru。sorekaramata放su。放shiteoitemata抑eru。七擒七縦孔明no軍略de攻metsukeru。約三十分kono順序wo繰ri返shite、身動kimo出来nakunattatokorowo見sumashitechoxtsuto口he啣ete振xtsute見ru。sorekaramata吐ki出su。今度ha地面no上he寝tagiri動kanaikara、kocchino手de突xtsu付ite、sono勢de飛bi上garutokorowomata抑etsukeru。koremoiyaninattekara、最後no手段toshitemushamusha食tteshimau。tsuidedakara蟷螂wo食xtsuta事nonai人ni話shiteokuga、蟷螂haamari旨i物dehanai。soushite滋養分mo存外少naiyoudearu。蟷螂狩rini次ide蝉取rito云u運動woyaru。単ni蝉to云ttatokoroga同ji物bakaridehanai。人間nimo油野郎、minmin野郎、oshiitsukutsuku野郎gaarugotoku、蝉nimo油蝉、minmin、oshiitsukutsukugaaru。油蝉hashitsukokute行kan。minminha横風de困ru。tada取xtsute面白inohaoshiitsukutsukudearu。koreha夏no末ninaranaito出te来nai。八tsu口no綻bikara秋風ga断warinashini膚wo撫detehakkusho風邪wo引itato云u頃熾ni尾wo掉ri立tetenaku。善ku鳴ku奴de、吾輩kara見ruto鳴kunoto猫nitorareruyorihokani天職ganaito思warerukuraida。秋no初hakoitsuwo取ru。korewo称shite蝉取ri運動to云u。choxtsuto諸君ni話shiteokugaiyashikumo蝉to名notsuku以上ha、地面no上ni転gattehaoran。地面no上ni落chiteirumononiha必zu蟻gatsuiteiru。吾輩no取runohakono蟻no領分ni寝転ndeiru奴dehanai。高i木no枝nitomaxtsute、oshiitsukutsukuto鳴iteiru連中wo捕erunodearu。koremotsuidedakara博学naru人間ni聞kitaigaarehaoshiitsukutsukuto鳴kunoka、tsukutsukuoshiito鳴kunoka、sono解釈次第niyotteha蝉no研究上少nakarazaru関係gaaruto思u。人間no猫ni優rutokorohakonnatokoroni存surunode、人間no自ra誇ru点momatakayouna点niarunodakara、今即答ga出来nainarayoku考eteoitarayokarou。mottomo蝉取ri運動上hadocchinishitemo差shi支ehanai。tada声woshirubeni木wo上xtsute行xtsute、先方ga夢中ninaxtsute鳴iteirutokorowounto捕erubakarida。korehamottomo簡略na運動ni見etenakanaka骨no折reru運動dearu。吾輩ha四本no足wo有shiteirukara大地wo行ku事nioitehaaete他no動物niha劣rutoha思wanai。少nakutomo二本to四本no数学的智識kara判断shite見te人間niha負kenaitsumoridearu。shikashi木登rini至tteha大分吾輩yori巧者na奴gairu。本職no猿ha別物toshite、猿no末孫taru人間nimonakanaka侮rubekarazaru手合gairu。元来ga引力ni逆ratteno無理na事業dakara出来nakutemo別段no恥辱toha思wankeredomo、蝉取ri運動上niha少nakarazaru不便wo与eru。幸ni爪to云u利器gaarunode、doukakouka登rihasurumonono、hatade見ruhodo楽dehagozaran。nominarazu蝉ha飛bumonodearu。蟷螂君to違xtsute一tabi飛ndeshimattaga最後、sekkakuno木登rimo、木登razuto何no択mutokoronashito云u悲運ni際会suru事ganaitomo限ran。最後ni時々蝉kara小便wokakerareru危険gaaru。ano小便gayayatomosuruto眼wo覘tteshoguttekuruyouda。逃gerunoha仕方ganaikara、douka小便bakariha垂renyouni致shitai。飛bu間際ni溺riwo仕runoha一体dou云u心理的状態no生理的器械ni及bosu影響darou。yaharisetsunasanoamarikashiran。aruiha敵no不意ni出dete、choxtsuto逃ge出su余裕wo作rutameno方便ka知ran。sousuruto烏賊no墨wo吐ki、beranme-no刺物wo見se、主人ga羅甸語wo弄suru類to同ji綱目ni入rubeki事項tonaru。koremo蝉学上忽kasenisubekarazaru問題dearu。充分研究surebakoredakedetashikani博士論文no価値haaru。soreha余事dakara、sonokurainishitemata本題ni帰ru。蝉nomottomo集注surunoha——集注gaokashikereba集合daga、集合ha陳腐dakarayahari集注nisuru。——蝉nomottomo集注surunoha青桐dearu。漢名wo梧桐to号surusouda。tokorogakono青桐ha葉ga非常ni多i、shikamosono葉ha皆団扇kuraina大sadearukara、彼等ga生i重naruto枝gamarude見enaikurai茂tteiru。koregahanahada蝉取ri運動no妨害ninaru。声hasuredomo姿ha見ezuto云u俗謡hatokuni吾輩notameni作xtsuta者dehanakaroukato怪shimarerukuraidearu。吾輩ha仕方ganaikaratada声wo知rubeni行ku。下kara一間bakarinotokorode梧桐ha注文通ri二叉ninatteirukara、kokode一休息shite葉裏kara蝉no所在地wo探偵suru。mottomokokomade来ruuchini、gasagasato音wo立tete、飛bi出su気早na連中gairu。一羽飛butomouikenai。真似wosuru点nioite蝉ha人間ni劣ranukurai馬鹿dearu。atokara続々飛bi出su。漸々二叉ni到着suru時分niha満樹寂toshite片声wotodomezaru事gaaru。katsutekokomade登xtsute来te、dokowodou見廻washitemo、耳wodou振ttemo蝉気ganainode、出直sunomo面倒dakarashibaraku休息shiyouto、叉no上ni陣取xtsute第二no機会wo待chi合seteitara、itsuno間nika眠kunaxtsute、tsui黒甜郷裡ni遊nda。oyato思xtsute眼ga醒metara、二叉no黒甜郷裡kara庭no敷石no上hedotarito落chiteita。shikashi大概ha登ru度ni一tsuha取xtsute来ru。tada興味no薄i事niha樹no上de口ni啣eteshimawanakutehanaran。dakara下he持xtsute来te吐ki出su時ha大方死ndeiru。ikurajarashitemo引xtsu掻itemo確然taru手答ganai。蝉取rino妙味hajixtsuto忍nde行tteoshii君ga一生懸命ni尻尾wo延bashitari縮mashitarishiteirutokorowo、waxtsuto前足de抑eru時niaru。kono時tsukutsuku君ha悲鳴wo揚gete、薄i透明na羽根wo縦横無尽ni振u。sono早i事、美事naru事ha言語道断、実ni蝉世界no一偉観dearu。余hatsukutsuku君wo抑eru度niitsudemo、tsukutsuku君ni請求shitekono美術的演芸wo見setemorau。soregaiyaninarutogo免wo蒙xtsute口no内he頬張tteshimau。蝉niyoruto口no内he這入ttemade演芸wotsuduketeirunogaaru。蝉取rino次niyaru運動ha松滑ridearu。koreha長kukaku必要monaikara、choxtsuto述beteoku。松滑rito云uto松wo滑ruyouni思ukamo知renga、soudehanaiyahari木登rino一種dearu。tada蝉取riha蝉wo取rutameni登ri、松滑riha、登ru事wo目的toshite登ru。korega両者no差dearu。元来松ha常磐nite最明寺no御馳走woshitekara以来今日ni至rumade、iyanigotsugotsushiteiru。従xtsute松no幹hodo滑ranaimonohanai。手懸rinoiimonohanai。足懸rinoiimonohanai。——換言sureba爪懸rinoiimonohanai。sono爪懸rinoii幹he一気呵成ni馳ke上ru。馳ke上tteoite馳ke下garu。馳ke下garuniha二法aru。一hasakasaninaxtsute頭wo地面he向kete下ritekuru。一ha上ttamamano姿勢wokuzusazuni尾wo下nishite降riru。人間ni問ugadocchigamuzukashiika知tteruka。人間noasahakana了見deha、douse降rirunodakara下向ni馳ke下riru方ga楽dato思udarou。sorega間違tteru。君等ha義経ga鵯越wo落toshitakotodakewo心得te、義経desae下wo向ite下rirunodakara猫nanzoha無論下ta向kidetakusandato思unodarou。sou軽蔑surumonodehanai。猫no爪hadocchihe向ite生eteiruto思u。minna後rohe折reteiru。soredakara鳶口noyouni物wokakete引ki寄seru事ha出来ruga、逆ni押shi出su力hanai。今吾輩ga松no木wo勢yoku馳ke登ttatosuru。suruto吾輩ha元来地上no者dearukara、自然no傾向kara云eba吾輩ga長ku松樹no巓ni留maruwo許sanni相違nai、tadaokeba必zu落chiru。shikashi手放shide落chiteha、amari早過giru。dakara何等kano手段womottekono自然no傾向wo幾分kayurumenakerebanaran。kore即chi降rirunodearu。落chirunoto降rirunoha大変na違noyoudaga、sono実思ttahodono事dehanai。落chirunowo遅kusuruto降rirunode、降rirunowo早kusuruto落chiru事ninaru。落chiruto降rirunoha、chitorino差dearu。吾輩ha松no木no上kara落chirunohaiyadakara、落chirunowo緩mete降rinakerebanaranai。即chiarumonowomoxtsute落chiru速度ni抵抗shinakerebanaran。吾輩no爪ha前申su通ri皆後ro向kidearukara、moshi頭wo上nishite爪wo立terebakono爪no力ha悉ku、落chiru勢ni逆xtsute利用出来ru訳dearu。従xtsute落chiruga変jite降riruninaru。実ni見易ki道理dearu。shikarunimata身wo逆nishite義経流ni松no木越woyaxtsute見給e。爪haattemo役niha立tan。zuruzuru滑xtsute、dokonimo自分no体量wo持chi答eru事ha出来nakunaru。kokonioitekasekkaku降riyouto企teta者ga変化shite落chiru事ninaru。kono通ri鵯越hamuzukashii。猫nouchidekono芸ga出来ru者ha恐raku吾輩nomidearou。soredakara吾輩hakono運動wo称shite松滑rito云unodearu。最後ni垣巡rinitsuite一言suru。主人no庭ha竹垣womoxtsute四角nishikirareteiru。椽側to平行shiteiru一片ha八九間moarou。左右ha双方共四間ni過gin。今吾輩no云xtsuta垣巡rito云u運動hakono垣no上wo落chinaiyouni一周surunodearu。korehayari損u事momamaaruga、首尾yoku行kutoo慰ninaru。kotoni所々ni根wo焼ita丸太ga立tteirukara、choxtsuto休息ni便宜gaaru。今日ha出来gayokattanode朝kara昼madeni三返yaxtsute見taga、yarutabiniumakunaru。umakunaru度ni面白kunaru。toutou四返繰ri返shitaga、四返目ni半分hodo巡rikaketara、隣no屋根kara烏ga三羽飛nde来te、一間bakari向uni列wo正shitetomaxtsuta。koreha推参na奴da。人no運動no妨wosuru、kotonidokono烏daka籍monai分在de、人no塀hetomarutoiu法gaarumonkato思ttakara、通rundaoi除kitamaeto声wokaketa。真先no烏hakocchiwo見teniyaniya笑tteiru。次noha主人no庭wo眺meteiru。三羽目ha嘴wo垣根no竹de拭iteiru。何ka食xtsute来tani違nai。吾輩ha返答wo待tsutameni、彼等ni三分間no猶予wo与ete、垣no上ni立tteita。烏ha通称wo勘左衛門to云usoudaga、naruhodo勘左衛門da。吾輩gaikura待ttetemo挨拶moshinakereba、飛bimoshinai。吾輩ha仕方ganaikara、sorosoro歩ki出shita。suruto真先no勘左衛門gachoito羽wo広geta。yaxtsuto吾輩no威光ni恐rete逃gerunato思ttara、右向kara左向ni姿勢wokaetadakedearu。kono野郎！　地面no上narasono分ni捨teokunodehanaiga、ikansen、tadasae骨no折reru道中ni、勘左衛門nadowo相手nishiteiru余裕ganai。toittemata立留maxtsute三羽ga立chi退kunowo待tsunomoiyada。第一sou待tteiteha足gatsudukanai。先方ha羽根noaru身分dearukara、konna所hehatomaritsuketeiru。従xtsute気ni入rebaitsumademo逗留surudarou。kocchihakorede四返目datadasae大分労reteiru。iwanya綱渡rinimo劣razaru芸当兼運動woyarunoda。何等no障害物ganakutesae落chintoha保証ga出来nnoni、konna黒装束ga、三個mo前途wo遮tteha容易narazaru不都合da。iyoiyotonareba自ra運動wo中止shite垣根wo下riruyori仕方ganai。面倒dakara、issosayou仕rouka、敵ha大勢no事dehaarushi、kotonihaamarikono辺niha見馴renu人体dearu。口嘴ga乙ni尖gaxtsute何daka天狗no啓shi子noyouda。douse質noii奴denainiha極tteiru。退却ga安全darou、amari深入riwoshite万一落chidemoshitaranaosara恥辱da。to思tteiruto左向woshita烏ga阿呆to云xtsuta。次nomo真似woshite阿呆to云xtsuta。最後no奴ha御鄭寧nimo阿呆阿呆to二声叫nda。ikani温厚naru吾輩demokoreha看過出来nai。第一自己no邸内de烏輩ni侮辱saretatoatteha、吾輩no名前nikakawaru。名前hamadanaikara係wariyouganakarouto云unara体面ni係waru。決shite退却ha出来nai。諺nimo烏合no衆to云ukara三羽daxtsute存外弱ikamo知renai。進merudake進meto度胸wo据ete、nosonoso歩ki出su。烏ha知ran顔woshite何ka御互ni話woshiteiru様子da。iyoiyo肝癪ni障ru。垣根no幅gamou五六寸moattarahidoi目ni合seteyarundaga、残念na事nihaikura怒ttemo、nosonosotoshikaarukarenai。youyakuno事先鋒wo去ru事約五六寸no距離made来temou一息dato思uto、勘左衛門ha申shi合setayouni、ikinari羽搏woshite一二尺飛bi上gaxtsuta。sono風ga突然余no顔wo吹ita時、haxtsuto思ttara、tsui踏mi外zushite、sutonto落chita。korehashikujittato垣根no下kara見上geruto、三羽共元no所nitomaxtsute上kara嘴wo揃ete吾輩no顔wo見下shiteiru。図太i奴da。睨metsuketeyattaga一向利kanai。背wo丸kushite、少々唸ttaga、masumasu駄目da。俗人ni霊妙naru象徴詩gawakaranugotoku、吾輩ga彼等ni向xtsute示su怒rino記号mo何等no反応wo呈出shinai。考ete見ruto無理nonaitokoroda。吾輩ha今made彼等wo猫toshite取ri扱tteita。sorega悪rui。猫narakonokuraiyarebatashikani応erunodaga生憎相手ha烏da。烏no勘公toaxtsute見reba致shi方ganai。実業家ga主人苦沙弥先生wo圧倒shiyoutoaserugotoku、西行ni銀製no吾輩wo進呈surugagotoku、西郷隆盛君no銅像ni勘公ga糞wohiruyounamonodearu。機wo見runi敏naru吾輩hatoutei駄目to見te取ttakara、奇麗sapparito椽側he引ki上geta。mou晩飯no時刻da。運動moiiga度wo過gosuto行kanu者de、karada全体ga何tonaku緊riganai、gutagutano感gaaru。nominarazumada秋no取ri付kide運動中ni照ri付kerareta毛goromoha、西日wo思u存分吸収shitato見ete、hotettetamaranai。毛穴kara染mi出su汗ga、流rerebato思unoni毛no根ni膏noyouninebari付ku。背中gamuzumuzusuru。汗demuzumuzusurunoto蚤ga這ttemuzumuzusurunoha判然to区別ga出来ru。口no届ku所nara噛mu事mo出来ru、足no達suru領分ha引ki掻ku事mo心得niaruga、脊髄no縦ni通u真中to来tara自分no及bu限denai。kou云u時niha人間wo見懸kete矢鱈nikosuri付keruka、松no木no皮de充分摩擦術wo行uka、二者sono一wo択banto不愉快de安眠mo出来兼neru。人間ha愚namonodearukara、猫nade声de——猫nade声ha人間no吾輩ni対shite出su声da。吾輩wo目安nishite考ereba猫nade声dehanai、naderare声dearu——yoroshii、tonikaku人間ha愚namonodearukara撫derare声de膝no傍he寄xtsute行kuto、大抵no場合nioite彼moshikuha彼女wo愛surumonoto誤解shite、waga為sumamani任serunomika折々ha頭sae撫detekurerumonoda。shikaruni近来吾輩no毛中ninomito号suru一種no寄生虫ga繁殖shitanode滅多ni寄ri添uto、必zu頸筋wo持xtsute向uhe抛ri出sareru。wazukani眼ni入ruka入ranuka、取runimo足ranu虫notameni愛想wotsukashitato見eru。手wo翻seba雨、手wo覆seba雲tohakono事da。高ganomino千疋ya二千疋deyokumaakonnani現金na真似ga出来tamonoda。人間世界wo通jite行wareru愛no法則no第一条nihakouarusouda。——自己no利益ninaru間ha、subekaraku人wo愛subeshi。——人間no取ri扱ga俄然豹変shitanode、ikura痒yukutemo人力wo利用suru事ha出来n。dakara第二no方法niyoxtsute松皮摩擦法woyaruyorihokani分別hanai。shikarabachottokosuxtsute参roukatomata椽側kara降rikaketaga、iyakoremo利害相償wanu愚策dato心付ita。to云unohahokademonai。松niha脂gaaru。kono脂tarusukoburu執着心no強i者de、moshi一tabi、毛no先hekuxtsu付keyoumononara、雷ga鳴ttemobaruchixtsuku艦隊ga全滅shitemo決shite離renai。shikanominarazu五本no毛hekobiritsukuga早ika、十本ni蔓延suru。十本yararetanato気ga付kuto、mou三十本引xtsu懸tteiru。吾輩ha淡泊wo愛suru茶人的猫dearu。konna、shitsukoi、毒悪na、nechinechishita、執念深i奴ha大嫌da。tatoi天下no美猫toiedomogo免蒙ru。iwanya松脂nioitewoyada。車屋no黒no両眼kara北風ni乗jite流reru目糞to択butokoronaki身分womoxtsute、kono淡灰色no毛衣wo大nashinisurutoha怪shikaran。少shiha考ete見rugaii。toittatokorodekyatsunakanaka考eru気遣hanai。ano皮noatarihe行xtsute背中wotsukeruga早ika必zubetaritooideninaruni極tteiru。konna無分別na頓痴奇wo相手nishiteha吾輩no顔ni係warunominarazu、引ite吾輩no毛並ni関suru訳da。ikura、muzumuzushitaxtsute我慢suruyorihokani致shi方haarumai。shikashikono二方法共実行出来ntonarutohanahada心細i。今nioite一工夫shiteokantoshimainihamuzumuzu、nechinechino結果病気ni罹rukamo知renai。何ka分別haarumaikanato、後to足wo折xtsute思案shitaga、futo思i出shita事gaaru。uchino主人ha時々手拭to石鹸womoxtsute飄然toizureheka出te行ku事gaaru、三四十分shite帰ttatokorowo見ruto彼no朦朧taru顔色ga少shiha活気wo帯bite、晴reyakani見eru。主人noyouna汚苦shii男nikonokuraina影響wo与erunara吾輩nihamou少shi利目gaaruni相違nai。吾輩hatadadesaekonokuraina器量dakara、koreyori色男ninaru必要hanaiyounamonono、万一病気ni罹xtsute一歳何ga月de夭折suruyouna事gaatteha天下no蒼生ni対shite申shi訳ganai。聞ite見rutokoremo人間nohima潰shini案出shita洗湯narumonodasouda。douse人間no作ttamonodakara碌namonodenainiha極tteirugakono際no事dakara試shini這入xtsute見runomoyokarou。yaxtsute見te功験ganakerebayosumadeno事da。shikashi人間ga自己notameni設備shita浴場he異類no猫wo入rerudakeno洪量gaarudarouka。korega疑問dearu。主人gasumashite這入rukurainotokorodakara、yomoya吾輩wo断waru事monakaroukeredomo万一o気no毒様wo食uyouna事gaatteha外聞gawarui。koreha一先zu容子wo見ni行kuni越shita事hanai。見ta上dekorenarayoito当riga付itara、手拭wo啣ete飛bi込nde見you。tokokomade思案wo定meta上denosonosoto洗湯he出掛keta。
　横町wo左he折reruto向uni高itoyo竹noyounamonoga屹立shite先kara薄i煙wo吐iteiru。kore即chi洗湯dearu。吾輩hasoxtsuto裏口kara忍bi込nda。裏口kara忍bi込munowo卑怯toka未練toka云uga、areha表karadenakuteha訪問suru事ga出来numonoga嫉妬半分ni囃shi立teru繰ri言dearu。昔kara利口na人ha裏口kara不意wo襲u事nikimatteiru。紳士養成方no第二巻第一章no五pe-jinisou出teirusouda。sono次nope-jiniha裏口ha紳士no遺書nishite自身徳wo得runo門naritoarukuraida。吾輩ha二十世紀no猫dakarakonokuraino教育haaru。anmari軽蔑shitehaikenai。sate忍bi込nde見ruto、左no方ni松wo割xtsute八寸kurainishitanoga山noyouni積ndeaxtsute、sono隣riniha石炭ga岡noyouni盛ttearu。naze松薪ga山noyoude、石炭ga岡noyoukato聞ku人gaarukamo知renaiga、別ni意味mo何monai、tadachoxtsuto山to岡wo使i分ketadakedearu。人間mo米wo食ttari、鳥wo食ttari、肴wo食ttari、獣wo食ttariiroirono悪mono食iwoshitsukushitaagekutsuini石炭made食uyouni堕落shitanoha不憫dearu。行ki当riwo見ruto一間hodono入口ga明ke放shininaxtsute、中wo覗kutogangaragannogaanto物静kadearu。sono向側de何kashikirini人間no声gasuru。iwayuru洗湯hakono声no発suru辺ni相違naito断定shitakara、松薪to石炭no間ni出来teru谷aiwo通ri抜kete左he廻xtsute、前進suruto右手ni硝子窓gaaxtsute、sonosotoni丸i小桶ga三角形即chipiramiddonogotoku積mikasanetearu。丸imonoga三角ni積marerunoha不本意千万darouto、hisokani小桶諸君no意wo諒toshita。小桶no南側ha四五尺no間板ga余xtsute、atakamo吾輩wo迎urumononogotoku見eru。板no高saha地面wo去ru約一me-torudakara飛bi上garuniha御誂eno上等dearu。yoroshiito云inagarahirarito身wo躍rasutoiwayuru洗湯ha鼻no先、眼no下、顔no前niburatsuiteiru。天下ni何ga面白ito云xtsute、未da食wazarumonowo食i、未da見zarumonowo見ruhodono愉快hanai。諸君mouchino主人nogotoku一週三度kurai、kono洗湯界ni三十分乃至四十分wo暮sunaraiiga、moshi吾輩nogotoku風呂to云umonowo見ta事ganainara、早ku見rugaii。親no死目ni逢wanakutemoiikara、koredakeha是非見物surugaii。世界広shitoiedomokonna奇観hamatatoarumai。
　何ga奇観da？　何ga奇観daxtsute吾輩hakorewo口nisuruwo憚karuhodono奇観da。kono硝子窓no中niujauja、gaagaa騒ideiru人間hakotogotoku裸体dearu。台湾no生蕃dearu。二十世紀noadamudearu。somosomo衣装no歴史wo繙keba——長i事dakarakorehatoiferusudorextsuku君ni譲xtsute、繙kudakehayameteyaruga、——人間ha全ku服装de持tterunoda。十八世紀no頃大英国basuno温泉場nioitebo-・nasshiga厳重na規則wo制定shita時nadoha浴場内de男女共肩kara足made着物dekakushitakuraidearu。今wo去ru事六十年前koremo英国no去ru都de図案学校wo設立shita事gaaru。図案学校no事dearukara、裸体画、裸体像no模写、模型wo買i込nde、koko、kashikoni陳列shitanohayokattaga、iza開校式wo挙行suru一段ninaxtsute当局者wo初me学校no職員ga大困却woshita事gaaru。開校式woyarutosureba、市no淑女wo招待shinakerebanaran。tokoroga当時no貴婦人方no考niyoruto人間ha服装no動物dearu。皮wo着ta猿no子分dehanaito思tteita。人間toshite着物wotsukenainoha象no鼻nakigagotoku、学校no生徒nakigagotoku、兵隊no勇気nakigagotoku全kusono本体wo失shiteiru。iyashikumo本体wo失shiteiru以上ha人間toshiteha通用shinai、獣類dearu。仮令模写模型niseyo獣類no人間to伍surunoha貴女no品位wo害suru訳dearu。dearimasukara妾等ha出席御断wari申suto云wareta。sokode職員共ha話senai連中datoha思ttaga、何shiro女ha東西両国wo通jite一種no装飾品dearu。米舂nimonaren志願兵nimonarenaiga、開校式niha欠kubekarazaru化装道具dearu。to云utokorokara仕方ganai、呉服屋he行xtsute黒布wo三十五反八分七買xtsute来te例no獣類no人間nikotogotoku着物wokiseta。失礼gaattehanaranto念ni念wo入rete顔made着物wokiseta。kayounishiteyouyakuno事滞rinaku式wosumashitato云u話gaaru。sonokurai衣服ha人間nitoxtsute大切namonodearu。近頃ha裸体画裸体画to云tteshikirini裸体wo主張suru先生moarugaarehaayamatteiru。生retekara今日ni至rumade一日mo裸体ninaxtsuta事ganai吾輩kara見ruto、doushitemo間違tteiru。裸体ha希臘、羅馬no遺風ga文芸復興時代no淫靡no風ni誘waretekara流行ridashitamonode、希臘人ya、羅馬人ha平常kara裸体wo見做reteitanodakara、korewomoxtsute風教上no利害no関係gaarunadotoha毫mo思i及banakattanodarouga北欧ha寒i所da。日本desae裸de道中ganarumonokato云ukuraidakara独逸ya英吉利de裸ninatteoreba死ndeshimau。死ndeshimattehatsumaranaikara着物wokiru。minnaga着物wokireba人間ha服装no動物ninaru。一tabi服装no動物tonaxtsuta後ni、突然裸体動物ni出逢eba人間toha認menai、獣to思u。soredakara欧洲人kotoni北方no欧洲人ha裸体画、裸体像womoxtsute獣toshite取ri扱tteiinodearu。猫ni劣ru獣to認定shiteiinodearu。美shii？　美shikutemo構wankara、美shii獣to見做sebaiinodearu。kou云uto西洋婦人no礼服wo見takato云umonomoarukamo知renaiga、猫no事dakara西洋婦人no礼服wo拝見shita事hanai。聞kutokoroniyoruto彼等ha胸woarawashi、肩woarawashi、腕woarawashitekorewo礼服to称shiteirusouda。怪shikaran事da。十四世紀頃madeha彼等no出de立chihashikaku滑稽dehanakaxtsuta、yahari普通no人間no着rumonowo着teoxtsuta。soreganazekonna下等na軽術師流ni転化shitekitakaha面倒dakara述benai。知ru人zo知ru、知ranumonoha知ran顔woshiteorebayoroshikarou。歴史hatonikaku彼等hakakaru異様na風態woshite夜間dakeha得々tarunimo係warazu内心ha少々人間rashiitokoromoaruto見ete、日ga出ruto、肩wosubomeru、胸wokakusu、腕wo包mu、dokomokashikomokotogotoku見enakushiteshimaunominarazu、足no爪一本demo人ni見serunowo非常ni恥辱to考eteiru。korede考etemo彼等no礼服narumonoha一種no頓珍漢的作用niyoxtsute、馬鹿to馬鹿no相談kara成立shitamonodato云u事ga分ru。sorega口惜shikereba日中demo肩to胸to腕wo出shiteite見rugaii。裸体信者dattesono通rida。sorehodo裸体gaiimononara娘wo裸体nishite、tsuideni自分mo裸ninaxtsute上野公園wo散歩demosurugaii、dekinai？　出来nainodehanai、西洋人gayaranaikara、自分moyaranainodarou。現nikono不合理極maru礼服wo着te威張xtsute帝国hoterunadohe出懸kerudehanaika。sono因縁wo尋neruto何nimonai。tada西洋人gakirukara、着ruto云umadeno事darou。西洋人ha強ikara無理demo馬鹿気teitemo真似nakerebayari切renainodarou。長imononiha捲karero、強imononiha折rero、重imononiha圧sareroto、sourero尽shideha気ga利kandehanaika。気ga利kandemo仕方ganaito云unara勘弁surukara、amari日本人woerai者to思ttehaikenai。学問toiedomosono通ridagakoreha服装ni関係ganai事dakara以下略tosuru。
　衣服hakakunogotoku人間nimo大事namonodearu。人間ga衣服ka、衣服ga人間kato云ukurai重要na条件dearu。人間no歴史ha肉no歴史niarazu、骨no歴史niarazu、血no歴史niarazu、単ni衣服no歴史dearuto申shitaikuraida。dakara衣服wo着kenai人間wo見ruto人間rashii感jigashinai。marude化物ni邂逅shitayouda。化物demo全体ga申shi合sete化物ninareba、iwayuru化物ha消etenakunaru訳dakara構wanga、soredeha人間自身ga大ni困却suru事ninarubakarida。sono昔shi自然ha人間wo平等narumononi製造shite世no中ni抛ri出shita。dakaradonna人間demo生rerutokiha必zu赤裸dearu。moshi人間no本性ga平等ni安nzurumononaraba、yoroshikukono赤裸nomamade生長shiteshikarubekidarou。shikaruni赤裸no一人ga云unihakou誰mo彼mo同jideha勉強suru甲斐ganai。骨wo折xtsuta結果ga見enu。doukashite、orehaoreda誰ga見temooredato云utokoroga目nitsukuyounishitai。sorenitsuiteha何ka人ga見teaxtsuto魂消ru物wokaradanitsukete見tai。何ka工夫haarumaikato十年間考eteyouyaku猿股wo発明shitesugusamakorewo穿ite、douda恐re入ttarouto威張ttesokoirawo歩ita。korega今日no車夫no先祖dearu。単簡naru猿股wo発明surunoni十年no長日月wo費yashitanohaisasaka異na感moaruga、soreha今日kara古代ni溯xtsute身wo蒙昧no世界ni置ite断定shita結論to云umonode、sono当時nikorekuraina大発明hanakattanodearu。dekarutoha「余ha思考su、故ni余ha存在su」toiu三tsu子nidemo分ruyouna真理wo考e出sunoni十何年ka懸ttasouda。subete考e出su時niha骨no折rerumonodearukara猿股no発明ni十年wo費yashitaxtsute車夫no智慧niha出来過giruto云wanebanarumai。saa猿股ga出来ruto世no中de幅nokikunoha車夫bakaridearu。amari車夫ga猿股wotsukete天下no大道wo我物顔ni横行濶歩surunowo憎rashiito思xtsute負ken気no化物ga六年間工夫shite羽織to云u無用no長物wo発明shita。suruto猿股no勢力ha頓ni衰ete、羽織全盛no時代tonaxtsuta。八百屋、生薬屋、呉服屋ha皆kono大発明家no末流dearu。猿股期、羽織期no後ni来runoga袴期dearu。koreha、何da羽織no癖nito癇癪wo起shita化物no考案ninattamonode、昔no武士今no官員nadoha皆kono種属dearu。kayouni化物共gawaremowaremoto異wo衒i新wo競xtsute、tsuiniha燕no尾nikatadoxtsuta畸形made出現shitaga、退itesono由来wo案zuruto、何mo無理矢理ni、出鱈目ni、偶然ni、漫然ni持chi上gaxtsuta事実deha決shitenai。皆勝chitai勝chitaino勇猛心no凝ttesamazamano新形tonattamonode、oreha手前janaizoto振retearuku代rini被tteirunodearu。shite見rutokono心理karashite一大発見ga出来ru。sorehahokademonai。自然ha真空wo忌mugotoku、人間ha平等wo嫌uto云u事da。sudeni平等wo嫌tteyamuwo得zu衣服wo骨肉nogotokukayounitsuke纏u今日nioite、kono本質no一部分taru、kore等wo打chiyaxtsute、元no杢阿弥no公平時代ni帰runoha狂人no沙汰dearu。yoshi狂人no名称wo甘njitemo帰ru事ha到底出来nai。帰xtsuta連中wo開明人no目kara見reba化物dearu。仮令世界何億万no人口wo挙gete化物no域ni引zurioroshitekorenara平等darou、minnaga化物dakara恥zukashii事hanaito安心shitemoyappari駄目dearu。世界ga化物ninaxtsuta翌日karamata化物no競争ga始maru。着物wotsukete競争ga出来nakereba化物naride競争woyaru。赤裸ha赤裸dedokomademo差別wo立tetekuru。kono点kara見temo衣服hatoutei脱gu事ha出来naimononinatteiru。
　shikaruni今吾輩ga眼下ni見下shita人間no一団体ha、kono脱gubekarazaru猿股mo羽織mo乃至袴mokotogotoku棚no上ni上gete、無遠慮nimo本来no狂態wo衆目環視no裡ni露出shite平々然to談笑wo縦manishiteiru。吾輩ga先刻一大奇観to云ttanohakono事dearu。吾輩ha文明no諸君子notamenikokoni謹ndesono一般wo紹介suruno栄wo有suru。
　何dakagochagochashiteite何nikara記述shiteiika分ranai。化物noyaru事niha規律ganaikara秩序立xtsuta証明wosurunoni骨ga折reru。mazu湯槽kara述beyou。湯槽daka何daka分ranaiga、大方湯槽toiumonodarouto思ubakaridearu。幅ga三尺kurai、長ha一間半moaruka、sorewo二tsuni仕切xtsute一tsuniha白i湯ga這入tteiru。何demo薬湯toka号surunodasoude、石灰wo溶kashi込ndayouna色ni濁tteiru。mottomotada濁tteirunodehanai。膏gixtsute、重ta気ni濁tteiru。yoku聞kuto腐xtsute見erunomo不思議hanai、一週間ni一度shika水wo易enainodasouda。sono隣riha普通一般no湯no由dagakorematamoxtsute透明、瑩徹nadotoha誓xtsute申sarenai。天水桶wo攪ki混zetakuraino価値hasono色no上nioite充分arawareteiru。korekaraga化物no記述da。大分骨ga折reru。天水桶no方ni、突xtsu立tteiru若造ga二人iru。立ttamama、向i合xtsute湯wozabuzabu腹no上hekaketeiru。ii慰mida。双方共色no黒i点nioite間然surutokoronakimadeni発達shiteiru。kono化物ha大分逞mashiinato見teiruto、yagate一人ga手拭de胸noatariwo撫de廻shinagara「金san、doumo、kokoga痛ndeikeneega何darou」to聞kuto金sanha「sorya胃sa、胃te云u奴ha命wotorukarane。用心shineetoabunaiyo」to熱心ni忠告wo加eru。「dattekono左no方daze」ta左肺no方wo指su。「sokoga胃daana。左ga胃de、右ga肺dayo」「soukana、oraamata胃hakokoirakato思xtsuta」to今度ha腰no辺wo叩ite見seruto、金sanha「sorya疝気daane」to云xtsuta。tokorohe二十五六no薄i髯wo生yashita男gadobunto飛bi込nda。suruto、karadani付iteita石鹸ga垢to共ni浮kiagaru。鉄気noaru水wo透kashite見ta時noyounikirakirato光ru。sono隣rini頭no禿geta爺sanga五分刈wo捕ete何ka弁jiteiru。双方共頭dake浮kashiteirunomida。「iyakou年wototteha駄目sane。人間moyakiga廻ccha若i者niha叶wanaiyo。shikashi湯dakeha今demo熱inodenaito心持ga悪kutene」「旦那nanka丈夫namonodesuze。sonokurai元気gaarya結構da」「元気monainosa。tada病気woshinaidakesa。人間ha悪i事saeshinakeryaa百二十madeha生kirumondakarane」「hee、sonnani生kirumondesuka」「生kirutomo百二十madeha受ke合u。御維新前牛込ni曲淵to云u旗本gaaxtsute、sokoniita下男ha百三十dattayo」「soitsuha、yoku生kitamondesune」「aa、anmari生ki過gitetsui自分no年wo忘retene。百madeha覚eteimashitagasorekara忘reteshimaimashitato云ttetayo。soredewashino知tteitanoga百三十no時dattaga、sorede死ndanjanai。sorekaradounattaka分ranai。事niyorutomada生kiterukamo知renai」to云inagara槽kara上ru。髯wo生yashiteiru男ha雲母noyounamonowo自分no廻rini蒔ki散rashinagara独rideniyaniya笑tteita。入re代xtsute飛bi込nde来tanoha普通一般no化物toha違xtsute背中ni模様画wohori付keteiru。岩見重太郎ga大刀wo振ri翳shite蟒wo退治rutokoronoyoudaga、惜shii事ni未da竣功no期ni達sennode、蟒hadokonimo見enai。従xtsute重太郎先生isasaka拍子抜keno気味ni見eru。飛bi込minagara「箆棒ni温ruiya」to云xtsuta。surutomata一人続ite乗ri込ndanoga「koryadoumo……mou少shi熱kunakucchaa」to顔woshikamenagara熱inowo我慢suru気色tomo見etaga、重太郎先生to顔wo見合sete「yaa親方」to挨拶wosuru。重太郎ha「yaa」to云ttaga、yagate「民sanhadoushitane」to聞ku。「doushitaka、janjanga好kidakarane」「janjanbakarijanee……」「soukai、ano男mo腹noyokunee男dakarane。——dou云umonka人ni好karenee、——dou云umonodaka、——doumo人ga信用shinee。職人teemonoha、annamonjaneega」「souyo。民sannanzaa腰ga低injanee、頭ga高keenda。soredakaradoumo信用sareneendane」「本当niyo。arede一ppashi腕gaarutsumoridakara、——tsumari自分no損daana」「白銀町nimo古i人ga亡kunattene、今ja桶屋no元santo煉瓦屋no大将to親方gureena者daana。kochitoraakoushitekokode生retamondaga、民sannanzaa、dokokara来tandaka分ryashinee」「souyo。shikashiyokuaredakeninattayo」「un。dou云umonka人ni好karenee。人ga交際waneekarane」to徹頭徹尾民sanwo攻撃suru。
　天水桶hakonokurainishite、白i湯no方wo見rutokorehamata非常na大入de、湯no中ni人ga這入tteruto云wanyori人no中ni湯ga這入tteruto云u方ga適当dearu。shikamo彼等hasukoburu悠々閑々taru物de、先刻kara這入rumonohaaruga出ru物ha一人monai。kou這入xtsuta上ni、一週間motometeoitara湯moyogoreruhazudato感心shitenaoyoku槽no中wo見渡suto、左no隅ni圧shitsukerarete苦沙弥先生ga真赤ninattesukundeiru。可哀souni誰ka路woakete出shiteyarebaiinonito思unoni誰mo動kisounimoshinakereba、主人mo出youtosuru気色mo見senai。tadajittoshite赤kunatteirubakaridearu。korehago苦労na事da。narubeku二銭五厘no湯銭wo活用shiyouto云u精神karashite、kayouni赤kunarunodarouga、早ku上garanto湯気niagarugato主思ino吾輩ha窓no棚kara少nakarazu心配shita。suruto主人no一軒置ite隣rini浮iteru男ga八no字wo寄senagara「korehachito利ki過giruyouda、doumo背中no方kara熱i奴gajirijiri湧itekuru」to暗ni列席no化物ni同情wo求meta。「naanikoregachoudoii加減desu。薬湯hakonokuraidenaito利kimasen。watashino国nazodehakono倍mo熱i湯he這入rimasu」to自慢rashiku説ki立terumonogaaru。「一体kono湯ha何ni利kundeshou」to手拭wo畳nde凸凹頭wokakushita男ga一同ni聞ite見ru。「iroironamononi利kimasuyo。何demoiiteendakarane。豪気daane」to云ttanoha瘠seta黄瓜noyouna色to形towo兼ne得taru顔no所有者dearu。sonnani利ku湯nara、mou少shiha丈夫souninaresounamonoda。「薬wo入re立teyori、三日目ka四日目gachoudoiiyoudesu。今日等ha這入ri頃desuyo」to物知ri顔ni述betanowo見ruto、膨re返xtsuta男dearu。koreha多分垢肥ridarou。「飲ndemo利kimashouka」todokokaraka知ranaiga黄色i声wo出su者gaaru。「冷eta後nadoha一杯飲nde寝ruto、奇体ni小便ni起kinaikara、maayaxtsute御覧nasai」to答etanoha、dono顔kara出ta声ka分ranai。
　湯槽no方hakoregurainishite板間wo見渡suto、iruwairuwa絵nimonaranaiadamugazurarito並nde各勝手次第na姿勢de、勝手次第natokorowo洗tteiru。sono中nimottomo驚rokubekinoha仰向keni寝te、高i明kari取wo眺meteirunoto、腹這ininaxtsute、溝no中wo覗ki込ndeiru両adamudearu。korehayohodo閑naadamuto見eru。坊主ga石壁wo向iteshagandeiruto後rokara、小坊主gashikirini肩wo叩iteiru。koreha師弟no関係上三介no代理wo務merunodearou。本当no三介moiru。風邪wo引itato見ete、konoatsuinonichanchanwo着te、小判形no桶karazaato旦那no肩he湯woabiseru。右no足wo見ruto親指no股ni呉絽no垢擦riwo挟ndeiru。kochirano方deha小桶wo慾張xtsute三tsu抱e込nda男ga、隣rino人ni石鹸wo使e使eto云inagarashikirini長談議woshiteiru。何darouto聞ite見rutokonna事wo言tteita。「鉄砲ha外国kara渡ttamondane。昔ha斬ri合ibakarisa。外国ha卑怯dakarane、soredeannamonoga出来tanda。doumo支那janeeyouda、yappari外国noyouda。和唐内no時nya無kattane。和唐内hayahari清和源氏sa。nandemo義経ga蝦夷kara満洲he渡xtsuta時ni、蝦夷no男de大変学nodekiru人gakuxtsu付ite行ttatee話shidane。soredesono義経nomusukoga大明wo攻metandaga大明ja困rukara、三代将軍he使woyokoshite三千人no兵隊wo借shitekureroto云uto、三代様gasoitsuwo留meteoite帰sanee。——何toka云ttaxtsuke。——何demo何toka云u使da。——soredesono使wo二年tometeoiteshimaini長崎de女郎wo見setandagane。sono女郎ni出来ta子ga和唐内sa。sorekara国he帰xtsute見ruto大明ha国賊ni亡bosareteita。……」何wo云unokasappari分ranai。sono後roni二十五六no陰気na顔woshita男ga、bonyarishite股no所wo白i湯deshikirinitadeteiru。腫物ka何kade苦shindeiruto見eru。sono横ni年no頃ha十七八de君toka僕toka生意気na事woberabera喋舌tterunohakono近所no書生darou。sonomata次ni妙na背中ga見eru。尻no中kara寒竹wo押shi込ndayouni背骨no節ga歴々to出teiru。soushitesono左右ni十六musashini似taru形ga四個zutsu行儀yoku並ndeiru。sono十六musashiga赤ku爛rete周囲ni膿womotteirunomoaru。kou順々ni書itekuruto、書ku事ga多過gite到底吾輩no手際nihasono一斑sae形容suru事ga出来n。koreha厄介na事woyari始meta者dato少々辟易shiteiruto入口no方ni浅黄木綿no着物wokita七十bakarino坊主ganuxtsuto見wareta。坊主ha恭shikukorerano裸体no化物ni一礼shite「hei、donata様mo、毎日相変razuarigatou存jimasu。今日ha少々御寒ugozaimasukara、douzo御緩kuri——douzo白i湯he出tari這入ttarishite、yururito御attamari下sai。——番頭sanya、douka湯加減woyoku見te上getena」toyodominaku述be立teta。番頭sanha「o-i」to答eta。和唐内ha「愛嬌monodane。aredenakuteha商買ha出来naiyo」to大ni爺sanwo激賞shita。吾輩ha突然kono異na爺sanni逢ttechoxtsuto驚roitakarakocchino記述hasonomamanishite、shibaraku爺sanwo専門ni観察suru事nishita。爺sanhayagate今上ri立teno四tsubakarino男no子wo見te「坊chan、kochiraheoide」to手wo出su。小供ha大福wo踏mi付ketayouna爺sanwo見te大変dato思ttaka、wa-xtsuto悲鳴wo揚getenaki出su。爺sanha少shiku不本意no気味de「iya、御泣kika、nani？　爺sanga恐i？　iya、korehakoreha」to感嘆shita。仕方ganaimonodakaratachimachi機鋒wo転jite、小供no親ni向xtsuta。「ya、koreha源san。今日ha少shi寒ina。yuube、近江屋he這入xtsuta泥棒ha何to云u馬鹿na奴jano。ano戸no潜rino所wo四角ni切ri破tteno。soushiteo前no。何mo取razuni行ndagena。御巡risanka夜番demo見etamonodearou」to大ni泥棒no無謀wo憫笑shitagamata一人wo捉ramaete「haihai御寒u。anata方ha、御若ikara、amario感jininarankano」to老人dakenitada一人寒gatteiru。
　shibarakuha爺sanno方he気wo取rarete他no化物no事ha全ku忘reteitanominarazu、苦shisounisukundeita主人sae記憶no中kara消e去xtsuta時突然流shito板no間no中間de大kina声wo出sumonogaaru。見ruto紛remonaki苦沙弥先生dearu。主人no声no図抜kete大inarunoto、sono濁xtsute聴ki苦shiinoha今日ni始maxtsuta事dehanaiga場所ga場所dakeni吾輩ha少karazu驚roita。koreha正shiku熱湯no中ni長時間noaida我慢woshite浸tteottatame逆上shitani相違naito咄嗟no際ni吾輩ha鑑定wotsuketa。soremo単ni病気no所為nara咎muru事monaiga、彼ha逆上shinagaramo充分本心wo有shiteiruni相違nai事ha、何notamenikono法外no胴間声wo出shitakawo話sebasuguwakaru。彼ha取runimo足ranu生意気書生wo相手ni大人気monai喧嘩wo始metanodearu。「moxtsuto下gare、oreno小桶ni湯ga這入tteikan」to怒鳴runoha無論主人dearu。物ha見youdedoudemonarumonodakara、kono怒号wotada逆上no結果tobakari判断suru必要hanai。万人nouchini一人kuraiha高山彦九郎ga山賊wo叱shitayoudakuraini解釈shitekurerukamo知ren。当人自身mosonotsumorideyaxtsuta芝居kamo分ranga、相手ga山賊womoxtsute自raoran以上ha予期suru結果ha出te来naini極tteiru。書生ha後rowo振ri返xtsute「僕hamotokarakokoniitanodesu」tootonashiku答eta。koreha尋常no答de、tadasono地wo去ranu事wo示shitadakega主人no思i通rininarannode、sono態度to云i言語to云i、山賊toshite罵ri返subekihodono事demonainoha、ikani逆上no気味no主人demo分tteiruhazuda。shikashi主人no怒号ha書生no席sonomonoga不平nanodehanai、先刻karakono両人ha少年ni似合wazu、iyani高慢chikina、利ita風no事bakari併beteitanode、始終sorewo聞kasareta主人ha、全kukono点ni立腹shitamonoto見eru。dakara先方deotonashii挨拶woshitemo黙xtsute板no間he上garihasen。今度ha「何da馬鹿野郎、人no桶he汚nai水wopichapicha跳nekasu奴gaaruka」to喝shi去xtsuta。吾輩mokono小僧wo少々心憎ku思tteitakara、kono時心中nihachoxtsuto快哉wo呼ndaga、学校教員taru主人no言動toshiteha穏kanaranu事to思uta。元来主人haamari堅過giteikan。石炭notaki殻見tayounikasakasashiteshikamoiyani硬i。mukashihannibarugaarupusu山wo超eru時ni、路no真中ni当xtsute大kina岩gaaxtsute、doushitemo軍隊ga通行上no不便邪魔wosuru。sokodehannibaruhakono大kina岩he醋wokakete火wo焚ite、柔kanishiteoite、sorekara鋸dekono大岩wo蒲鉾noyouni切xtsute滞rinaku通行woshitasouda。主人nogotokukonna利目noaru薬湯he煮daruhodo這入ttemo少shimo功能nonai男hayahari醋wokakete火炙rinisuruni限ruto思u。shikarazunba、konna書生ga何百人出te来te、何十年kakattaxtsute主人no頑固ha癒rikkonai。kono湯槽ni浮iteirumono、kono流shinigorogoroshiteirumonoha文明no人間ni必要na服装wo脱gi棄teru化物no団体dearukara、無論常規常道womoxtsute律suru訳nihaikan。何woshitaxtsute構wanai。肺no所ni胃ga陣取xtsute、和唐内ga清和源氏ninaxtsute、民sanga不信用demoyokarou。shikashi一tabi流shiwo出te板no間ni上gareba、mou化物dehanai。普通no人類no生息suru娑婆he出tanoda、文明ni必要naru着物wokirunoda。従xtsute人間rashii行動wotoranakerebanaranhazudearu。今主人ga踏ndeirutokoroha敷居dearu。流shito板no間no境niaru敷居no上deaxtsute、当人hakorekara歓言愉色、円転滑脱no世界ni逆戻riwoshiyouto云u間際dearu。sono間際desurakakunogotoku頑固dearunara、kono頑固ha本人nitoxtsute牢toshite抜kubekarazaru病気ni相違nai。病気nara容易ni矯正suru事ha出来mai。kono病気wo癒su方法ha愚考niyorutotada一tsuaru。校長ni依頼shite免職shite貰u事即chikorenari。免職ninareba融通no利kanu主人no事dakarakixtsuto路頭ni迷uni極tteru。路頭ni迷u結果hanotare死niwoshinakerebanaranai。換言suruto免職ha主人nitoxtsute死no遠因ninarunodearu。主人ha好nde病気woshite喜kondeirukeredo、死nunoha大嫌dearu。死nanai程度nioite病気to云u一種no贅沢gashiteitainodearu。soredakarasonnani病気woshiteiruto殺suzoto嚇kaseba臆病naru主人no事dakarabiribirito悸e上garuni相違nai。kono悸e上garu時ni病気ha奇麗ni落chirudarouto思u。soredemo落chinakerebasoremadeno事sa。
　ikani馬鹿demo病気demo主人ni変rihanai。一飯君恩wo重nzuto云u詩人moaru事dakara猫daxtsute主人no身no上wo思wanai事haarumai。気no毒dato云u念ga胸一杯ninattatame、tsuisochirani気ga取rarete、流shino方no観察wo怠tatteiruto、突然白i湯槽no方面ni向xtsute口々ni罵ru声ga聞eru。kokonimo喧嘩ga起ttanokato振ri向kuto、狭i柘榴口ni一寸no余地monaikuraini化物ga取ritsuite、毛noaru脛to、毛nonai股to入ri乱rete動iteiru。折kara初秋no日ha暮ruruninannantoshite流shino上ha天井made一面no湯気ga立te籠meru。kano化物no犇ku様gasono間kara朦朧to見eru。熱i熱ito云u声ga吾輩no耳wo貫nuite左右he抜keruyouni頭no中de乱re合u。sono声niha黄nanomo、青inomo、赤inomo、黒inomoaruga互ni畳narikakaxtsute一種名状subekarazaru音響wo浴場内ni漲rasu。tada混雑to迷乱towo形容suruni適shita声to云unomide、hokaniha何no役nimo立tanai声dearu。吾輩ha茫然toshitekono光景ni魅入raretabakari立chisukundeita。yagatewa-wa-to云u声ga混乱no極度ni達shite、koreyorihamou一歩mo進menuto云u点made張ri詰merareta時、突然無茶苦茶ni押shi寄se押shi返shiteiru群no中kara一大長漢ganuxtsuto立chi上gaxtsuta。彼no身no丈wo見ruto他no先生方yorihatashikani三寸kuraiha高i。nominarazu顔kara髯ga生eteirunoka髯no中ni顔ga同居shiteirunoka分ranai赤tsurawo反ri返shite、日盛rini破re鐘wotsukuyouna声wo出shite「umeroumero、熱i熱i」to叫bu。kono声tokono顔bakariha、kano紛々to縺re合u群衆no上ni高ku傑出shite、sono瞬間niha浴場全体gakono男一人ninattato思waruruhododearu。超人da。ni-chenoiwayuru超人da。魔中no大王da。化物no頭梁da。to思xtsute見teiruto湯槽no後rodeo-ito答etamonogaaru。oyatomatamosochirani眸wosorasuto、暗憺toshite物色mo出来nu中ni、例nochanchan姿no三介ga砕keyoto一塊rino石炭wo竈no中ni投ge入rerunoga見eta。竈no蓋wokuguxtsute、kono塊rigapachipachito鳴rutokini、三介no半面gapaxtsuto明rukunaru。同時ni三介no後roniaru煉瓦no壁ga暗wo通shite燃erugotoku光xtsuta。吾輩ha少々物凄kunattakara早々窓kara飛bi下rite家ni帰ru。帰rinagaramo考eta。羽織wo脱gi、猿股wo脱gi、袴wo脱ide平等ninarouto力meru赤裸々no中niha、mata赤裸々no豪傑ga出te来te他no群小wo圧倒shiteshimau。平等haikurahadakaninattaxtsute得rarerumonodehanai。
　帰xtsute見ruto天下ha太平namonode、主人ha湯上garino顔woteratera光rashite晩餐wo食tteiru。吾輩ga椽側kara上garunowo見te、nonkina猫danaa、今頃dokowoaruiteirundarouto云xtsuta。膳no上wo見ruto、銭nonai癖ni二三品御菜wonarabeteiru。sonouchini肴no焼itanoga一疋aru。koreha何to称suru肴ka知ranga、何demo昨日atari御台場近辺deyararetani相違nai。肴ha丈夫namonodato説明shiteoitaga、ikura丈夫demokou焼karetari煮raretarishitehatamaran。多病nishite残喘wo保tsu方gayohodo結構da。kou考ete膳no傍ni坐xtsute、隙gaattara何ka頂戴shiyouto、見rugotoku見zarugotoku装tteita。konna装i方wo知ranaimonohatouteiumai肴ha食enaito諦menakerebaikenai。主人ha肴wochoxtsuto突ttsuitaga、umakunaito云u顔付woshite箸wo置ita。正面ni控etaru妻君hakoremata無言nomama箸no上下ni運動suru様子、主人no両顎no離合開闔no具合wo熱心ni研究shiteiru。
「oi、sono猫no頭wochoxtsuto撲xtsute見ro」to主人ha突然細君ni請求shita。
「撲teba、dousurundesuka」
「doushitemoiikarachoxtsuto撲xtsute見ro」
　koudesukato細君ha平手de吾輩no頭wochoxtsuto敲ku。痛kumo何tomonai。
「鳴kanjanaika」
「ee」
「mou一返yaxtsute見ro」
「何返yattaxtsute同ji事jaarimasenka」to細君mata平手depokato参ru。yahari何tomonaikara、jittoshiteita。shikashisono何notametaruyaha智慮深ki吾輩niha頓to了解shi難i。korega了解出来reba、doukakouka方法moarougatada撲xtsute見rodakara、撲tsu細君mo困rushi、撲tareru吾輩mo困ru。主人ha二度made思i通rininarannode、少々焦re気味de「oi、choxtsuto鳴kuyounibuxtsute見ro」to云xtsuta。
　細君ha面倒na顔付de「鳴kashite何ninasarundesuka」to問inagara、matapisharitooideninaxtsuta。kou先方no目的gawakareba訳hanai、鳴itesaeyareba主人wo満足saseru事ha出来runoda。主人hakakunogotoku愚物dakara厭ninaru。鳴kaserutamenara、tameto早ku云eba二返mo三返mo余計na手数hashinakutemosumushi、吾輩mo一度de放免ninaru事wo二度mo三度mo繰ri返esareru必要hanainoda。tada打xtsute見roto云u命令ha、打tsu事sore自身wo目的tosuru場合nohokani用ubekimonodenai。打tsunoha向uno事、鳴kunohakocchino事da。鳴ku事wo始mekara予期shite懸xtsute、tada打tsuto云u命令nouchini、kocchino随意tarubeki鳴ku事sae含matteruyouni考erunoha失敬千万da。他人no人格wo重nzento云umonoda。猫wo馬鹿nishiteiru。主人no蛇蝎nogotoku嫌u金田君narayarisouna事daga、赤裸々womoxtsute誇ru主人toshitehasukoburu卑劣dearu。shikashi実notokoro主人hakorehodokechina男dehanainodearu。dakara主人nokono命令ha狡猾no極ni出detanodehanai。tsumari智慧no足rinaitokorokara湧ita孑孑noyounamonoto思惟suru。飯wo食eba腹ga張runi極matteiru。切reba血ga出runi極tteiru。殺seba死nuni極matteiru。soredakara打teba鳴kuni極tteiruto速断woyattandarou。shikashisorehao気no毒daga少shi論理ni合wanai。sono格de行kuto川he落chireba必zu死nu事ninaru。天麩羅wo食eba必zu下痢suru事ninaru。月給womoraeba必zu出勤suru事ninaru。書物wo読meba必zuerakunaru事ninaru。必zusounatteha少shi困ru人ga出来tekuru。打teba必zunakanakerebanarantonaruto吾輩ha迷惑dearu。目白no時no鐘to同一ni見傚sareteha猫to生reta甲斐ganai。mazu腹no中dekoredake主人wo凹mashiteoite、shikaru後nya-to注文通ri鳴iteyaxtsuta。
　suruto主人ha細君ni向xtsute「今鳴ita、nyaato云u声ha感投詞ka、副詞ka何daka知tteruka」to聞ita。
　細君haamari突然na問nanode、何nimo云wanai。実wo云uto吾輩mokoreha洗湯no逆上gamadasamenaitamedarouto思ttakuraida。元来kono主人ha近所合壁有名na変人de現niaru人hatashikani神経病datomade断言shitakuraidearu。tokoroga主人no自信haeraimonode、orega神経病janai、世no中no奴ga神経病dato頑張tteiru。近辺nomonoga主人wo犬々to呼buto、主人ha公平wo維持surutame必要datoka号shite彼等wo豚々to呼bu。実際主人hadokomademo公平wo維持surutsumorirashii。困ttamonoda。kou云u男dakarakonna奇問wo細君ni対xtsute呈出surunomo、主人ni取tteha朝食前no小事件kamo知renaiga、聞ku方kara云waserutochoxtsuto神経病ni近i人no云isouna事da。dakara細君ha煙ni捲kareta気味de何tomo云wanai。吾輩ha無論何tomo答eyouganai。suruto主人hatachimachi大kina声de
「oi」to呼bikaketa。

　他人nara酒no上de云ubeki事wo、正気de云tteirutokorogasukoburu奇観dearu。mottomo今夜ni限xtsute酒wo無暗ninomu。平生nara猪口ni二杯tokimeteirunowo、mou四杯飲nda。二杯demo随分赤kunarutokorowo倍飲ndanodakara顔ga焼火箸noyounihotextsute、samo苦shisouda。soredemomadayamenai。「mou一杯」to出su。細君haamarino事ni

八

　垣巡rito云u運動wo説明shita時ni、主人no庭wo結i繞rashitearu竹垣no事wochoxtsuto述betatsumoridearuga、kono竹垣no外gasugu隣家、即chi南隣no次郎chantokoto思tteha誤解dearu。家賃ha安igasokoha苦沙弥先生dearu。与cchanya次郎channadoto号suru、iwayuruchan付kino連中to、薄xtsu片na垣一重wo隔tete御隣ri同志no親密naru交際ha結ndeoranu。kono垣no外ha五六間no空地deaxtsute、sono尽kurutokoroni檜ga蓊然to五六本併ndeiru。椽側kara拝見suruto、向uha茂xtsuta森de、kokoni往mu先生ha野中no一軒家ni、無名no猫wo友nishite日月wo送ru江湖no処士dearukanogotoki感gaaru。但shi檜no枝ha吹聴surugotoku密生shiteorannode、sono間kara群鶴館toiu、名前dake立派na安下宿no安屋根ga遠慮naku見erukara、shikaku先生wo想像surunonihayohodo骨no折rerunoha無論dearu。shikashikono下宿ga群鶴館nara先生no居hatashikani臥竜窟kuraina価値haaru。名前ni税hakakarankara御互nierasouna奴wo勝手次第ni付keru事toshite、kono幅五六間no空地ga竹垣wo添ute東西ni走ru事約十間、sorekara、tachimachi鉤no手ni屈曲shite、臥竜窟no北面wo取ri囲ndeiru。kono北面ga騒動no種dearu。本来nara空地wo行ki尽shitemataaki地、toka何toka威張ttemoiikuraini家no二側wo包ndeirunodaga、臥竜窟no主人ha無論窟内no霊猫taru吾輩surakonoaki地niha手kozutteiru。南側ni檜ga幅wo利kashiteirugotoku、北側niha桐no木ga七八本行列shiteiru。mou周囲一尺kuraininobiteirukara下駄屋sae連retekurebaii価ninarundaga、借家no悲shisaniha、ikura気ga付itemo実行ha出来n。主人ni対shitemo気no毒dearu。sendaxtsute学校no小使ga来te枝wo一本切xtsute行ttaga、sonotsugini来ta時ha新rashii桐no俎下駄wo穿ite、kono間no枝dekoshiraemashitato、聞kimosennoni吹聴shiteita。zurui奴da。桐haaruga吾輩及bi主人家族nitotteha一文nimonaranai桐dearu。玉wo抱ite罪arito云u古語gaarusoudaga、koreha桐wo生yashite銭nashito云ttemoshikarubekimonode、iwayuru宝no持chi腐redearu。愚narumonoha主人niarazu、吾輩niarazu、家主no伝兵衛dearu。inaikana、inaikana、下駄屋hainaikanato桐no方de催促shiteirunoni知ran面woshite屋賃bakari取ri立tenikuru。吾輩ha別ni伝兵衛ni恨monaikara彼no悪口wokonokurainishite、本題ni戻ttekono空地ga騒動no種dearuto云u珍譚wo紹介仕ruga、決shite主人niittehaikenai。koregirino話shidearu。somosomokono空地ni関shite第一no不都合naru事ha垣根nonai事dearu。吹ki払i、吹ki通shi、抜ke裏、通行御免天下晴reteno空地dearu。aruto云uto嘘wotsukuyoudeyoroshikunai。実wo云utoattanodearu。shikashi話shiha過去he溯ranto源因ga分karanai。源因ga分karanaito、医者demo処方ni迷惑suru。dakarakokohe引ki越shite来ta当時karayukkurito話shi始meru。吹ki通shimo夏haseiseishite心持chigaiimonoda、不用心daxtsute金nonaitokoroni盗難noaruhazuhanai。dakara主人no家ni、arayuru塀、垣、乃至ha乱杭、逆茂木no類ha全ku不要dearu。shikashinagarakoreha空地no向uni住居suru人間moshikuha動物no種類如何niyoxtsute決seraruru問題dearouto思u。従ttekono問題wo決surutameniha勢i向u側ni陣取tteiru君子no性質wo明kanisenkerebanaran。人間daka動物daka分ranai先ni君子to称surunohahanahada早計noyoudehaaruga大抵君子de間違hanai。梁上no君子nadoto云xtsute泥棒sae君子to云u世no中dearu。但shikono場合niokeru君子ha決shite警察no厄介ninaruyouna君子dehanai。警察no厄介ninaranai代rini、数dekonashita者to見ete沢山iru。ujaujairu。落雲館to称suru私立no中学校——八百no君子woiyaga上ni君子ni養成surutameni毎月二円no月謝wo徴集suru学校dearu。名前ga落雲館dakara風流na君子bakarikato思uto、soregasomosomono間違ninaru。sono信用subekarazaru事ha群鶴館ni鶴no下rizarugotoku、臥竜窟ni猫gairuyounamonodearu。学士toka教師toka号surumononi主人苦沙弥君nogotoki気違noaru事wo知xtsuta以上ha落雲館no君子ga風流漢bakaridenaito云u事gawakaru訳da。soregawakaranto主張surunaramazu三日bakari主人nouchihe宿rini来te見rugaii。
　前申sugotoku、kokohe引ki越shino当時ha、例no空地ni垣ganainode、落雲館no君子ha車屋no黒nogotoku、nosonosoto桐畠ni這入ri込ndekite、話wosuru、弁当wo食u、笹no上ni寝転bu——iroirono事woyattamonoda。sorekaraha弁当no死骸即chi竹no皮、古新聞、aruiha古草履、古下駄、furuto云u名notsukumonowo大概kokohe棄tetayouda。無頓着naru主人ha存外平気ni構ete、別段抗議mo申shi込mazuni打chi過gitanoha、知ranakattanoka、知ttemo咎mentsumorideattanoka分ranai。tokoroga彼等諸君子ha学校de教育wo受kuruni従xtsute、dandan君子rashikunattamonoto見ete、次第ni北側kara南側no方面he向kete蚕食wo企datete来ta。蚕食to云u語ga君子ni不似合narayametemoyoroshii。但shihokani言葉ganainodearu。彼等ha水草wo追ute居wo変zuru沙漠no住民nogotoku、桐no木wo去xtsute檜no方ni進nde来ta。檜noaru所ha座敷no正面dearu。yohodo大胆naru君子denakerebakorehodono行動ha取renhazudearu。一両日no後彼等no大胆hasarani一層no大wo加ete大々胆tonaxtsuta。教育no結果hodo恐shiimonohanai。彼等ha単ni座敷no正面ni逼runominarazu、kono正面nioite歌woutaidashita。何to云u歌ka忘reteshimattaga、決shite三十一文字no類dehanai、moxtsuto活溌de、moxtsuto俗耳ni入ri易i歌deaxtsuta。驚roitanoha主人bakaridehanai、吾輩mademo彼等君子no才芸ni嘆服shite覚ezu耳wo傾ketakuraidearu。shikashi読者mogo案内dearouga、嘆服to云u事to邪魔to云u事ha時toshite両立suru場合gaaru。kono両者gakono際図razumo合shite一tonattanoha、今kara考ete見temo返su返su残念dearu。主人mo残念deattarouga、yamuwo得zu書斎kara飛bi出shite行xtsute、kokoha君等no這入ru所dehanai、出給eto云xtsute、二三度追i出shitayouda。tokoroga教育noaru君子no事dakara、konna事deotonashiku聞ku訳ganai。追i出sarerebasugu這入ru。這入reba活溌naru歌woutau。高声ni談話wosuru。shikamo君子no談話dakara一風違xtsute、omeedano知raneenoto云u。sonna言葉ha御維新前ha折助to雲助to三助no専門的知識ni属shiteitasoudaga、二十世紀ninattekara教育aru君子no学bu唯一no言語dearusouda。一般kara軽蔑seraretaru運動ga、kakunogotoku今日歓迎seraruruyouninattanoto同一no現象dato説明shita人gaaru。主人hamata書斎kara飛bi出shitekono君子流no言葉nimottomo堪能naru一人wo捉maete、nazekokohe這入rukato詰問shitara、君子hatachimachi「omee、知ranee」no上品na言葉wo忘rete「kokoha学校no植物園kato思imashita」tosukoburu下品na言葉de答eta。主人ha将来wo戒mete放shiteyaxtsuta。放shiteyarunoha亀no子noyoudeokashiiga、実際彼ha君子no袖wo捉ete談判shitanodearu。konokuraiyakamashiku云ttaramouyokarouto主人ha思tteitasouda。tokoroga実際ha女※氏no時代kara予期to違umonode、主人hamata失敗shita。今度ha北側kara邸内wo横断shite表門kara抜keru、表門wogararitoakerukara御客kato思uto桐畠no方de笑u声gasuru。形勢hamasumasu不穏dearu。教育no功果haiyoiyo顕著ninattekuru。気no毒na主人hakoitsuha手ni合wanto、sorekara書斎he立te籠xtsute、恭shiku一書wo落雲館校長ni奉xtsute、少々御取締woto哀願shita。校長mo鄭重naru返書wo主人ni送xtsute、垣wosurukara待ttekureto云xtsuta。shibarakusuruto二三人no職人ga来te半日bakarino間ni主人no屋敷to、落雲館no境ni、高sa三尺bakarino四tsu目垣ga出来上gaxtsuta。koredeyouyou安心dato主人ha喜konda。主人ha愚物dearu。konokuraino事de君子no挙動no変化suru訳ganai。
　全体人nikarakaunoha面白imonodearu。吾輩noyouna猫desura、時々ha当家no令嬢nikarakaxtsute遊bukuraidakara、落雲館no君子ga、気no利kanai苦沙弥先生nikarakaunoha至極mottomonatokorode、koreni不平nanoha恐raku、karakawareru当人dakedearou。karakauto云u心理wo解剖shite見ruto二tsuno要素gaaru。第一karakawareru当人ga平気desumashiteitehanaran。第二karakau者ga勢力nioite人数nioite相手yori強kunakutehaikan。kono間主人ga動物園kara帰xtsute来teshikirini感心shite話shita事gaaru。聞ite見ruto駱駝to小犬no喧嘩wo見tanodasouda。小犬ga駱駝no周囲wo疾風nogotoku廻転shite吠e立teruto、駱駝ha何no気motsukazuni、依然toshite背中he瘤wokoshiraete突xtsu立ttamamadearusouda。ikura吠etemo狂ttemo相手nisennode、shimainiha犬mo愛想wotsukashiteyameru、実ni駱駝ha無神経dato笑tteitaga、soregakono場合no適例dearu。ikurakarakaumonoga上手demo相手ga駱駝to来teha成立shinai。sarebato云xtsute獅子ya虎noyouni先方ga強過gitemo者ninaran。karakaikakeruya否ya八tsu裂kinisareteshimau。karakauto歯womuki出shite怒ru、怒ru事ha怒ruga、kocchiwodousuru事mo出来naito云u安心noaru時ni愉快ha非常ni多imonodearu。nazekonna事ga面白ito云utosono理由hairoiroaru。mazuhimatsubushini適shiteiru。退屈na時niha髯no数sae勘定shite見takunaru者da。昔shi獄ni投zerareta囚人no一人ha無聊noamari、房no壁ni三角形wo重nete画itesono日wokurashitato云u話gaaru。世no中ni退屈hodo我慢no出来nikuimonohanai、何ka活気wo刺激suru事件ganaito生kiteirunogatsuraimonoda。karakauto云unomotsumarikono刺激wo作xtsute遊bu一種no娯楽dearu。但shi多少先方wo怒raseruka、jiraseruka、弱raserukashinakuteha刺激ninarankara、昔shikarakarakauto云u娯楽ni耽rumonoha人no気wo知ranai馬鹿大名noyouna退屈no多i者、moshikuha自分nonagusami以外ha考uruni暇nakihodo頭no発達ga幼稚de、shikamo活気no使i道ni窮suru少年kani限tteiru。次niha自己no優勢na事wo実地ni証明surumononihamottomo簡便na方法dearu。人wo殺shitari、人wo傷ketari、mataha人wo陥retarishitemo自己no優勢na事ha証明出来ru訳dearuga、korerahamushiro殺shitari、傷ketari、陥retarisurunoga目的notokiniyorubeki手段de、自己no優勢naru事hakono手段wo遂行shita後ni必然no結果toshite起ru現象ni過gin。dakara一方niha自分no勢力ga示shitakuxtsute、shikamosonnani人ni害wo与etakunaito云u場合niha、karakaunoga一番御恰好dearu。多少人wo傷kenakereba自己noerai事ha事実no上ni証拠daterarenai。事実ninaxtsute出te来naito、頭nouchide安心shiteitemo存外快楽nousuimonodearu。人間ha自己wo恃mumonodearu。否恃mi難i場合demo恃mitaimonodearu。soredakara自己hakoredake恃meru者da、korenara安心dato云u事wo、人ni対shite実地ni応用shite見naito気gasumanai。shikamo理窟nowakaranai俗物ya、amari自己ga恃mininarisoumonakute落chitsukinonai者ha、arayuru機会wo利用shite、kono証券wo握routosuru。柔術使ga時々人wo投gete見takunarunoto同ji事dearu。柔術no怪shiimonoha、douka自分yori弱i奴ni、tadano一返deiikara出逢xtsute見tai、素人demo構wanaikara抛gete見taito至極危険na了見wo抱ite町内woarukunomokoregatamedearu。sono他nimo理由hairoiroaruga、amari長kunarukara略suru事ni致su。聞kitakereba鰹節no一折mo持xtsute習inikurugaii、itsudemo教eteyaru。以上ni説kutokorowo参考shite推論shite見ruto、吾輩no考deha奥山no猿to、学校no教師gakarakauniha一番手頃dearu。学校no教師womoxtsute、奥山no猿ni比較shiteha勿体nai。——猿ni対shite勿体nainodehanai、教師ni対shite勿体nainodearu。shikashiyoku似teirukara仕方ganai、御承知no通ri奥山no猿ha鎖de繋gareteiru。ikura歯womuki出shitemo、kyakkyaxtsu騒idemo引ki掻kareru気遣hanai。教師ha鎖de繋gareteoranai代rini月給de縛rareteiru。ikurakarakattaxtsute大丈夫、辞職shite生徒wobunnaguru事hanai。辞職wosuru勇気noaruyounamononara最初kara教師nadowoshite生徒no御守riha勤menaihazudearu。主人ha教師dearu。落雲館no教師dehanaiga、yahari教師ni相違nai。karakauniha至極適当de、至極安直de、至極無事na男dearu。落雲館no生徒ha少年dearu。karakau事ha自己no鼻wo高kusuru所以de、教育no功果toshite至当ni要求shiteshikarubeki権利tomade心得teiru。nominarazukarakaidemoshinakereba、活気ni充chita五体to頭脳wo、ikani使用shiteshikarubekika十分no休暇中持teamashite困tteiru連中dearu。korerano条件ga備wareba主人ha自karakarakaware、生徒ha自karakarakau、誰kara云washitemo毫mo無理nonaitokorodearu。sorewo怒ru主人ha野暮no極、間抜no骨頂deshou。korekara落雲館no生徒gaikani主人nikarakattaka、koreni対shite主人gaikani野暮wo極metakawo逐一kaitego覧ni入reru。
　諸君ha四tsu目垣tohaikanaru者dearuka御承知dearou。風通shinoii、簡便na垣dearu。吾輩nadoha目no間kara自由自在ni往来suru事ga出来ru。koshiraetaxtsute、koshiraenakutaxtsute同ji事da。然shi落雲館no校長ha猫notameni四tsu目垣wo作ttanodehanai、自分ga養成suru君子ga潜rarentameni、wazawaza職人wo入rete結i繞rasetanodearu。naruhodoikura風通shigayoku出来teitemo、人間niha潜resouninai。kono竹womoxtsute組mi合setaru四寸角no穴wonukeru事ha、清国no奇術師張世尊sono人toiedomomuzukashii。dakara人間ni対shiteha充分垣no功能wotsukushiteiruni相違nai。主人gasono出来上ttanowo見te、korenarayokarouto喜ndanomo無理hanai。shikashi主人no論理niha大naru穴gaaru。kono垣yorimo大inaru穴gaaru。呑舟no魚womo洩rasubeki大穴gaaru。彼ha垣ha踰yubekimononiarazutono仮定kara出立shiteiru。iyashikumo学校no生徒taru以上haikani粗末no垣demo、垣to云u名gatsuite、分界線no区域sae判然sureba決shite乱入sareru気遣hanaito仮定shitanodearu。次ni彼hasono仮定woshibaraku打chi崩shite、yoshi乱入suru者gaattemo大丈夫to論断shitanodearu。四tsu目垣no穴wo潜ri得ru事ha、ikanaru小僧toiedomotoutei出来ru気遣hanaikara乱入no虞ha決shitenaito速定shiteshimattanodearu。naruhodo彼等ga猫denai限rihakono四角no目wonuketekuru事hashimai、shitakutemo出来maiga、乗ri踰eru事、飛bi越eru事ha何no事monai。kaextsute運動ninaxtsute面白ikuraidearu。
　垣no出来ta翌日kara、垣no出来nu前to同様ni彼等ha北側no空地hepokaripokarito飛bi込mu。但shi座敷no正面madeha深入riwoshinai。moshi追i懸keraretara逃gerunoni、少々himagairukara、予me逃geru時間wo勘定ni入rete、捕eraruru危険nonai所de遊弋woshiteiru。彼等ga何woshiteiruka東no離reniiru主人niha無論目ni入ranai。北側no空地ni彼等ga遊弋shiteiru状態ha、木戸woakete反対no方角kara鉤no手ni曲xtsute見ruka、mataha後架no窓kara垣根越shini眺meruyorihokani仕方ganai。窓kara眺meru時hadokoni何gairuka、一目明瞭ni見渡su事ga出来ruga、yoshiya敵wo幾人見出shitakarato云xtsute捕eru訳niha行kanu。tada窓no格子no中kara叱ritsukerubakaridearu。moshi木戸kara迂回shite敵地wo突koutosureba、足音wo聞kitsukete、pokaripokarito捉maru前ni向u側he下riteshimau。膃肭臍gahinatabokkowoshiteirutokorohe密猟船ga向ttayouna者da。主人ha無論後架de張ri番woshiteiru訳dehanai。to云xtsute木戸wo開ite、音gashitara直gu飛bi出su用意monai。moshisonna事woyaru日niha教師wo辞職shite、sono方専門ninaranakereba追ttsukanai。主人方no不利wo云uto書斎karaha敵no声dake聞ete姿ga見enainoto、窓karaha姿ga見erudakede手ga出senai事dearu。kono不利wo看破shitaru敵hakonna軍略wo講jita。主人ga書斎ni立te籠tteiruto探偵shita時niha、narubeku大kina声wo出shitewaawaa云u。sono中niha主人wohiyakasuyouna事wo聞koeyogashini述beru。shikamosono声no出所wo極mete不分明nisuru。choxtsuto聞kuto垣no内de騒ideirunoka、aruiha向u側deabareteirunoka判定shinikuiyounisuru。moshi主人ga出懸kete来tara、逃ge出suka、mataha始mekara向u側niite知ran顔wosuru。mata主人ga後架he——吾輩ha最前karashikirini後架後架tokitanai字wo使用surunowo別段no光栄tomo思tteoran、実ha迷惑千万dearuga、kono戦争wo記述suru上nioite必要dearukarayamuwo得nai。——即chi主人ga後架hemakari越shitato見te取rutokiha、必zu桐no木no附近wo徘徊shitewazato主人no眼nitsukuyounisuru。主人gamoshi後架kara四隣ni響ku大音wo揚gete怒鳴ritsukereba敵ha周章teru気色monaku悠然to根拠地he引kiageru。kono軍略wo用irareruto主人hahanahada困却suru。tashikani這入tteirunato思ttesutekkiwo持xtsute出懸keruto寂然toshite誰moinai。inaikato思xtsute窓karanozokuto必zu一二人這入tteiru。主人ha裏he廻xtsute見tari、後架kara覗ite見tari、後架kara覗ite見tari、裏he廻xtsute見tari、何度言ttemo同ji事daga、何度云ttemo同ji事wo繰ri返shiteiru。奔命ni疲rerutohakono事dearu。教師ga職業dearuka、戦争ga本務dearukachoxtsuto分ranaikurai逆上shite来ta。kono逆上no頂点ni達shita時ni下no事件ga起ttanodearu。
　事件ha大概逆上kara出ru者da。逆上toha読nde字nogotoku逆kasani上runodearu、kono点ni関shitehage-renmoparaserusasumo旧弊naru扁鵲mo異議wo唱uru者ha一人monai。tadadokohe逆kasani上rukaga問題dearu。mata何ga逆kasani上rukaga議論noarutokorodearu。古来欧洲人no伝説niyoruto、吾人no体内niha四種no液ga循環shiteottasouda。第一ni怒液to云u奴gaaru。korega逆kasani上ruto怒ri出su。第二ni鈍液to名dukurunogaaru。korega逆kasani上ruto神経ga鈍kunaru。次niha憂液、koreha人間wo陰気nisuru。最後ga血液、koreha四肢wo壮nnisuru。sono後人文ga進muni従xtsute鈍液、怒液、憂液haitsuno間nikanakunaxtsute、現今ni至tteha血液dakega昔noyouni循環shiteiruto云u話shida。dakaramoshi逆上suru者gaaraba血液yorihokanihaarumaito思wareru。shikarunikono血液no分量ha個人niyottechanto極matteiru。性分niyoxtsute多少no増減haaruga、mazu大抵一人前ni付五升五合no割合dearu。daniyoxtsute、kono五升五合ga逆kasani上ruto、上ttatokorodakeha熾nni活動suruga、sono他no局部ha欠乏wo感jite冷takunaru。choudo交番焼打no当時巡査gakotogotoku警察署he集xtsute、町内niha一人monakunattayounamonoda。aremo医学上kara診断wosuruto警察no逆上to云u者dearu。dekono逆上wo癒yasuniha血液wo従前nogotoku体内no各部he平均ni分配shinakerebanaran。sousuruniha逆kasani上xtsuta奴wo下he降sanakutehanaran。sono方nihairoiroaru。今ha故人tonararetaga主人no先君nadoha濡re手拭wo頭niatete炬燵niatatteoraretasouda。頭寒足熱ha延命息災no徴to傷寒論nimo出teiru通ri、濡re手拭ha長寿法nioite一日mo欠kubekarazaru者dearu。soredenakereba坊主no慣用suru手段wo試mirugayoi。一所不住no沙門雲水行脚no衲僧ha必zu樹下石上wo宿tosutoaru。樹下石上toha難行苦行notamedehanai。全kunobosewo下gerutameni六祖ga米wo舂kinagara考e出shita秘法dearu。試mini石no上ni坐ttego覧、尻ga冷erunoha当ri前darou。尻ga冷eru、nobosega下garu、koremata自然no順序nishite毫mo疑wo挟mubeki余地hanai。kayouniiroirona方法wo用itenobosewo下geru工夫ha大分発明saretaga、madanobosewo引ki起su良方ga案出sarenainoha残念dearu。一概ni考erutonoboseha損axtsute益naki現象dearuga、soubakari速断shitenaran場合gaaru。職業niyoruto逆上hayohodo大切na者de、逆上sento何nimo出来nai事gaaru。sono中demottomo逆上wo重nzurunoha詩人dearu。詩人ni逆上ga必要naru事ha汽船ni石炭ga欠kubekarazaruyouna者de、kono供給ga一日demo途切reruto彼re等ha手wo拱ite飯wo食uyorihokani何等no能monai凡人ninatteshimau。mottomo逆上ha気違no異名de、気違ninaranaito家業ga立chi行kantoatteha世間体ga悪ikara、彼等no仲間deha逆上wo呼buni逆上no名womotteshinai。申shi合seteinsupire-shon、insupire-shontosamo勿体souni称eteiru。koreha彼等ga世間wo瞞着surutameni製造shita名desono実ha正ni逆上dearu。pure-to-ha彼等no肩wo持ttekono種no逆上wo神聖naru狂気to号shitaga、ikura神聖demo狂気deha人ga相手nishinai。yahariinsupire-shonto云u新発明no売薬noyouna名wo付keteoku方ga彼等notameniyokarouto思u。shikashi蒲鉾no種ga山芋dearugotoku、観音no像ga一寸八分no朽木dearugotoku、鴨南蛮no材料ga烏dearugotoku、下宿屋no牛鍋ga馬肉dearugotokuinsupire-shonmo実ha逆上dearu。逆上deaxtsute見reba臨時no気違dearu。巣鴨he入院sezuni済munoha単ni臨時気違dearukarada。tokorogakono臨時no気違wo製造suru事ga困難nanodearu。一生涯no狂人hakaextsute出来安iga、筆wo執xtsute紙ni向u間dake気違nisurunoha、ikani巧者na神様demoyohodo骨ga折reruto見ete、nakanaka拵ete見senai。神ga作ttekuren以上ha自力de拵enakerebanaran。sokode昔kara今日made逆上術momata逆上torinoke術to同jiku大ni学者no頭脳wo悩mashita。aru人hainsupire-shonwo得rutameni毎日渋柿wo十二個zutsu食xtsuta。koreha渋柿wo食eba便秘suru、便秘sureba逆上ha必zu起rutoiu理論kara来tamonoda。mataaru人hakan徳利wo持xtsute鉄砲風呂he飛bi込nda。湯no中de酒wo飲ndara逆上suruni極tteiruto考etanodearu。sono人no説niyorutokorede成功shinakereba葡萄酒no湯wowakashite這入reba一返de功能gaaruto信ji切tteiru。shikashi金ganainodetsuini実行suru事ga出来nakute死ndeshimattanoha気no毒dearu。最後ni古人no真似woshitarainsupire-shonga起rudarouto思itsuita者gaaru。korehaaru人no態度動作wo真似ruto心的状態mosono人ni似tekuruto云u学説wo応用shitanodearu。酔pparainoyouni管wo捲iteiruto、itsuno間nika酒飲minoyouna心持ninaru、坐禅woshite線香一本no間我慢shiteirutodokotonaku坊主rashii気分ninareru。dakara昔karainsupire-shonwo受keta有名no大家no所作wo真似reba必zu逆上suruni相違nai。聞kutokoroniyorebayu-go-ha快走船no上he寝転nde文章no趣向wo考etasoudakara、船he乗xtsute青空wo見tsumeteireba必zu逆上受合dearu。suchi-vunsonha腹這ni寝te小説wo書itasoudakara、打tsu伏shininaxtsute筆wo持tebakixtsuto血ga逆kasani上ttekuru。kayouniiroirona人gairoirono事wo考e出shitaga、mada誰mo成功shinai。mazu今日notokorodeha人為的逆上ha不可能no事tonatteiru。残念daga致shi方ganai。早晩随意niinsupire-shonwo起shi得ru時機no到来suruha疑monai事de、吾輩ha人文notamenikono時機no一日mo早ku来ran事wo切望surunodearu。
　逆上no説明hakonokuraide充分darouto思ukara、koreyoriiyoiyo事件ni取rikakaru。shikashisubeteno大事件no前niha必zu小事件ga起rumonoda。大事件nomiwo述bete、小事件wo逸surunoha古来kara歴史家no常ni陥ru弊竇dearu。主人no逆上mo小事件ni逢u度ni一層no劇甚wo加ete、tsuini大事件wo引ki起shitanodearukarashite、幾分kasono発達wo順序立tete述benaito主人gaikani逆上shiteiruka分rinikui。分rinikuito主人no逆上ha空名ni帰shite、世間karahayomoyasorehododemonakarouto見kubirarerukamo知renai。sekkaku逆上shitemo人kara天晴na逆上to謡warenakuteha張ri合ganaidarou。korekara述beru事件ha大小ni係razu主人ni取xtsute名誉na者dehanai。事件sono物ga不名誉dearunaraba、責mete逆上naritomo、正銘no逆上deaxtsute、決shite人ni劣rumonodenaito云u事wo明kanishiteokitai。主人ha他ni対shite別nikoreto云xtsute誇runi足ru性質wo有shiteoran。逆上demo自慢shinakutehahokani骨wo折xtsute書ki立teteyaru種ganai。
　落雲館ni群garu敵軍ha近日ni至xtsute一種nodamudamu弾wo発明shite、十分no休暇、moshikuha放課後ni至xtsute熾ni北側no空地ni向xtsute砲火wo浴bisekakeru。konodamudamu弾ha通称wobo-ruto称ete、擂粉木no大kina奴womoxtsute任意korewo敵中ni発射suru仕掛dearu。ikuradamudamudaxtsute落雲館no運動場kara発射surunodakara、書斎ni立te籠tteru主人ni中ru気遣hanai。敵toiedomo弾道noamari遠過girunowo自覚sen事hanainodakeredo、sokoga軍略dearu。旅順no戦争nimo海軍kara間接射撃wo行xtsute偉大na功wo奏shitato云u話deareba、空地hekorogari落tsurubo-rutoiedomo相当no功果wo収me得nu事hanai。iwanya一発wo送ru度ni総軍力wo合setewa-to威嚇性大音声wo出sunioitewoyadearu。主人ha恐縮no結果toshite手足ni通u血管ga収縮sezaruwo得nai。煩悶no極sokoirawo迷付iteiru血ga逆sani上ruhazudearu。敵no計hanakanaka巧妙to云uteyoroshii。昔shi希臘niisukirasuto云u作家gaattasouda。kono男ha学者作家ni共通naru頭wo有shiteitato云u。吾輩noiwayuru学者作家ni共通naru頭toha禿to云u意味dearu。naze頭ga禿gerukato云eba頭no営養不足de毛ga生長suruhodo活気ganaikarani相違nai。学者作家hamottomo多ku頭wo使umonodeaxtsute大概ha貧乏ni極tteiru。dakara学者作家no頭haminna営養不足deminna禿geteiru。sateisukirasumo作家dearukara自然no勢禿genakutehanaran。彼hatsurutsuru然taru金柑頭wo有shiteoxtsuta。tokorogaaru日no事、先生例no頭——頭ni外行mo普段着monaikara例no頭ni極tteruga——sono例no頭wo振ri立te振ri立te、太陽ni照rashitsukete往来woaruiteita。korega間違inomotodearu。禿ge頭wo日niatete遠方kara見ruto、大変yoku光rumonoda。高i木niha風gaataru、光karu頭nimo何kaataranakutehanaran。kono時isukirasuno頭no上ni一羽no鷲ga舞tteitaga、見rutodokokade生捕xtsuta一疋no亀wo爪no先ni攫ndamamadearu。亀、supponnadoha美味ni相違naiga、希臘時代kara堅i甲羅wotsuketeiru。ikura美味demo甲羅tsukidehadousuru事mo出来n。海老no鬼殻焼haaruga亀no子no甲羅煮ha今desaenaikuraidakara、当時ha無論nakattani極tteiru。sasugano鷲mo少々持te余shita折柄、遥kano下界nipikato光xtsuta者gaaru。sono時鷲hashimetato思xtsuta。ano光ttamonono上he亀no子wo落shitanara、甲羅ha正shiku砕keruni極wamaxtsuta。砕ketaatokara舞i下rite中味wo頂戴sureba訳hanai。soudasoudato覗wo定mete、kano亀no子wo高i所kara挨拶mo無ku頭no上he落shita。生憎作家no頭no方ga亀no甲yori軟rakadeattamonodakara、禿hamechamechani砕kete有名naruisukirasuhakokoni無惨no最後wo遂geta。sorehasouto、解shikanerunoha鷲no了見dearu。例no頭wo、作家no頭to知xtsute落shitanoka、mataha禿岩to間違ete落shitamonoka、解決shiyou次第de、落雲館no敵tokono鷲towo比較suru事mo出来rushi、mata出来nakumonaru。主人no頭haisukirasunosorenogotoku、mata御歴々no学者nogotokupikapika光ttehaoran。shikashi六畳敷niseyoiyashikumo書斎to号suru一室wo控ete、居眠riwoshinagaramo、muzukashii書物no上he顔wo翳su以上ha、学者作家no同類to見傚sanakerebanaran。sousuruto主人no頭no禿geteorannoha、mada禿gerubeki資格ganaikarade、sono内ni禿gerudaroutoha近々kono頭no上ni落chikakarubeki運命dearou。shite見reba落雲館no生徒gakono頭wo目懸kete例nodamudamu丸wo集注surunoha策nomottomo時宜ni適shitamonoto云wanebanaran。moshi敵gakono行動wo二週間継続surunaraba、主人no頭ha畏怖to煩悶notame必zu営養no不足wo訴ete、金柑tomo薬缶tomo銅壺tomo変化surudarou。nao二週間no砲撃wo食eba金柑ha潰reruni相違nai。薬缶ha洩runi相違nai。銅壺narahibiga入runikimatteiru。kono睹易ki結果wo予想sende、akumademo敵to戦闘wo継続shiyouto苦心surunoha、tada本人taru苦沙弥先生nomidearu。
　aru日no午後、吾輩ha例nogotoku椽側he出te午睡woshite虎ninaxtsuta夢wo見teita。主人ni鶏肉wo持xtsute来ito云uto、主人gaheeto恐ru恐ru鶏肉wo持xtsute出ru。迷亭ga来takara、迷亭ni雁ga食itai、雁鍋he行xtsute誂raete来ito云uto、蕪no香no物to、塩煎餅toisshoni召shi上garimasuto雁no味ga致shimasuto例nogotoku茶羅xtsu鉾wo云ukara、大kina口woaite、u-to唸xtsute嚇shiteyattara、迷亭ha蒼kunaxtsute山下no雁鍋ha廃業致shimashitagaikaga取ri計imashoukato云xtsuta。sorenara牛肉de勘弁surukara早ku西川he行ttero-suwo一斤取xtsute来i、早kusento貴様kara食i殺suzoto云ttara、迷亭ha尻wo端折xtsute馳ke出shita。吾輩ha急nikaradaga大kikunattanode、椽側一杯ni寝sobextsute、迷亭no帰runowo待chi受keteiruto、tachimachi家中ni響ku大kina声gashitesekkakuno牛mo食wanu間ni夢gasamete吾ni帰xtsuta。suruto今made恐ru恐ru吾輩no前ni平伏shiteitato思inohokano主人ga、ikinari後架kara飛bi出shite来te、吾輩no横腹woiyato云uhodo蹴takara、oyato思uuchi、tachimachi庭下駄wotsukkakete木戸kara廻xtsute、落雲館no方hekakete行ku。吾輩ha虎kara急ni猫to収縮shitanodakara何tonaku極riga悪kumoari、okashikumoattaga、主人nokono権幕to横腹wo蹴rareta痛satode、虎no事hasugu忘reteshimaxtsuta。同時ni主人gaiyoiyo出馬shite敵to交戦suruna面白iwaito、痛inowo我慢shite、後wo慕xtsute裏口he出ta。同時ni主人ganusuttouto怒鳴ru声ga聞eru、見ruto制帽wotsuketa十八九ninaru倔強na奴ga一人、四tsu目垣wo向uhe乗ri越etsutsuaru。yaa遅kattato思uuchi、彼no制帽ha馳ke足no姿勢wotoxtsute根拠地no方he韋駄天nogotoku逃gete行ku。主人hanusuttouga大ni成功shitanode、matamonusuttouto高ku叫binagara追ikakete行ku。shikashikano敵ni追itsukutameniha主人no方de垣wo越sanakerebanaran。深入riwosureba主人自raga泥棒ninaruhazudearu。前申su通ri主人ha立派naru逆上家dearu。kou勢ni乗jitenusuttouwo追i懸keru以上ha、夫子自身ganusuttouni成ttemo追i懸kerutsumorito見ete、引ki返su気色monaku垣no根元made進nda。今一歩de彼hanusuttouno領分ni入ranakerebanaranto云u間際ni、敵軍no中kara、薄i髯wo勢naku生yashita将官ganokonokoto出馬shite来ta。両人ha垣wo境ni何ka談判shiteiru。聞ite見rutokonnatsumaranai議論dearu。
